<!-- &#9552;&#9552; URL پاکردنەوە: ?m=1 بەبێ redirect لادەبرێت &#9552;&#9552; -->
<script type="text/javascript">
  //<![CDATA[
  (function(){
    try{
      var loc = window.location;
      if(!loc.search) return;
      var params = new URLSearchParams(loc.search);
      if(!params.has('m')) return;
      params.delete('m');
      var newSearch = params.toString();
      var clean = loc.pathname + (newSearch ? '?' + newSearch : '') + loc.hash;
      history.replaceState(null, '', clean);
    }catch(e){}
  })();
  //]]>
  </script>

<!-- VideoObject + BreadcrumbList + WebPage JSON-LD (Single Post, JS Injection) -->
<script type="text/javascript">
  //<![CDATA[
  (function(){
    function _ld(obj){
      var s=document.createElement('script');
      s.type='application/ld+json';
      s.text=JSON.stringify(obj);
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    }
    var LOGO='https://i.ibb.co/DPpB0WX6/1000308715.jpg';
    var PUBLISHER={'@type':'Organization','name':'کوڕی پاک','logo':{'@type':'ImageObject','url':LOGO}};

    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){
      var cn=document.querySelector('link[rel="canonical"]');
      var url=cn?cn.href:location.href;
      var titleEl=document.querySelector('.post-title-main, h1.post-title');
      var descEl=document.querySelector('meta[name="description"]');
      var pubEl=document.querySelector('meta[property="article:published_time"]');
      var imgEl=document.querySelector('meta[property="og:image"]');
      var postTitle=titleEl?titleEl.textContent.trim():'';
      var desc=descEl?descEl.getAttribute('content'):postTitle;
      var pubDate=pubEl?pubEl.getAttribute('content'):new Date().toISOString();
      var thumb=imgEl?imgEl.getAttribute('content'):LOGO;

      /* ══ BreadcrumbList ══ */
      var items=[];var pos=1;
      items.push({'@type':'ListItem','position':pos++,'name':'کوڕی پاک','item':'https://kuripak2026.blogspot.com/'});
      var labelEl=document.querySelector('.post-labels a');
      if(labelEl) items.push({'@type':'ListItem','position':pos++,'name':labelEl.textContent.trim(),'item':labelEl.href});
      if(titleEl) items.push({'@type':'ListItem','position':pos,'name':postTitle,'item':url});
      if(items.length>=2){
        _ld({'@context':'https://schema.org','@type':'BreadcrumbList','itemListElement':items});
      }

      /* ══ WebPage Schema (هەموو پۆستێک) ══ */
      if(postTitle){
        _ld({
          '@context':'https://schema.org',
          '@type':'WebPage',
          'name':postTitle,
          'description':desc,
          'url':url,
          'inLanguage':'ckb',
          'isPartOf':{'@type':'WebSite','name':'کوڕی پاک','url':'https://kuripak2026.blogspot.com/'},
          'publisher':PUBLISHER,
          'datePublished':pubDate||undefined
        });
      }

      /* ══ VideoObject — YouTube ══ */
      var ytFrame=document.querySelector('.post-body iframe[src*="youtube"],.post-body iframe[src*="youtu.be"]');
      if(ytFrame){
        var vsrc=ytFrame.src||ytFrame.getAttribute('src')||'';
        var m=vsrc.match(/(?:embed\/|v=|youtu\.be\/)([A-Za-z0-9_-]{11})/);
        if(m){
          var vid=m[1];
          _ld({
            '@context':'https://schema.org',
            '@type':'VideoObject',
            'name':postTitle,
            'description':desc,
            'thumbnailUrl':'https://i.ytimg.com/vi/'+vid+'/maxresdefault.jpg',
            'uploadDate':pubDate,
            'embedUrl':'https://www.youtube.com/embed/'+vid,
            'contentUrl':'https://www.youtube.com/watch?v='+vid,
            'url':url,
            'inLanguage':'ckb',
            'publisher':PUBLISHER
          });
        }
      }

      /* ══ VideoObject — Vidmol ══ */
      var vmFrame=document.querySelector('.post-body iframe[src*="vidmol"]');
      if(vmFrame){
        var vmsrc=vmFrame.src||vmFrame.getAttribute('src')||'';
        _ld({
          '@context':'https://schema.org',
          '@type':'VideoObject',
          'name':postTitle,
          'description':desc,
          'thumbnailUrl':thumb,
          'uploadDate':pubDate,
          'embedUrl':vmsrc,
          'url':url,
          'inLanguage':'ckb',
          'publisher':PUBLISHER
        });
      }
    });
  })();
  //]]>
  </script>

<nav class="blog-pager">
<a href="https://kuripak2026.blogspot.com/?m=1" id="kp-newer-url" style="display:none"></a>
<a href="https://kuripak2026.blogspot.com/search?updated-max=2026-04-02T11:52:00-07:00&amp;max-results=6&amp;m=1" id="kp-older-url" style="display:none"></a>
<div id="kp-pagination"><a href="https://kuripak2026.blogspot.com/?m=1" class="kp-page-btn nav-btn"><i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-right"></i></a><span class="kp-page-btn active">1</span><a href="https://kuripak2026.blogspot.com/search?updated-max=2026-04-02T11:52:00-07:00&amp;max-results=6&amp;m=1" class="kp-page-btn">2</a><span class="kp-page-btn disabled">3</span><a href="https://kuripak2026.blogspot.com/search?updated-max=2026-04-02T11:52:00-07:00&amp;max-results=6&amp;m=1" class="kp-page-btn nav-btn"><i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-left"></i></a></div>
</nav>
<script>
//<![CDATA[
(function(){
  var MAX_RESULTS = 6; // ژمارەی پۆستی هەر پەڕەیەک — لەگەڵ Blogger max-results بگونجێنە

  // بەدەست هێنانی blogId لە URL ئێستا
  var blogId = '';
  var scripts = document.querySelectorAll('script');
  for(var i=0;i<scripts.length;i++){
    var m = (scripts[i].textContent||'').match(/'blogId':\s*'(\d+)'/);
    if(m){blogId=m[1];break;}
  }

  // بەدەست هێنانی پەڕەی ئێستا لە URL
  function getCurrentPage(){
    var url = window.location.href;
    // label pages: /search/label/X?updated-max=...&start=N
    var sm = url.match(/[?&]start=(\d+)/);
    if(sm) return Math.floor(parseInt(sm[1])/MAX_RESULTS)+1;
    // homepage/older pages: updated-max param
    var om = url.match(/updated-max=([^&]+)/);
    if(!om) return 1; // پەڕەی یەکەم
    return null; // پێویستە لە Feed بزانین
  }

  var newerEl = document.getElementById('kp-newer-url');
  var olderEl = document.getElementById('kp-older-url');
  var newerUrl = newerEl ? newerEl.getAttribute('href') : null;
  var olderUrl = olderEl ? olderEl.getAttribute('href') : null;

  // فیدی Blogger بۆ ژمارەی کۆی پۆستەکان
  var feedBase = 'https://' + window.location.hostname + '/feeds/posts/default';
  
  // بەدەست هێنانی label ئەگەر هەیە
  var labelMatch = window.location.href.match(/\/search\/label\/([^?&]+)/);
  var labelParam = labelMatch ? '/-/' + decodeURIComponent(labelMatch[1]) : '';
  var countUrl = feedBase + labelParam + '?max-results=1&alt=json';

  fetch(countUrl)
    .then(function(r){return r.json();})
    .then(function(data){
      var total = parseInt(data.feed.openSearch$totalResults.$t)||0;
      var totalPages = Math.ceil(total/MAX_RESULTS);
      if(totalPages<1)totalPages=1;

      // پەڕەی ئێستا دیاری بکە
      var curPage = 1;
      if(!newerUrl && olderUrl) curPage = 1; // یەکەم پەڕە
      else if(newerUrl && !olderUrl) curPage = totalPages; // کۆتا پەڕە
      else if(newerUrl && olderUrl){
        // ناوەندی — پێویستە URL بخوێنینەوە
        var sm2 = window.location.href.match(/[?&]start=(\d+)/);
        if(sm2) curPage = Math.floor(parseInt(sm2[1])/MAX_RESULTS)+1;
        else {
          // updated-max based: ژمارەی پۆستی پێش ئەم پەڕەیە بژمێرین
          var updatedMax = window.location.href.match(/updated-max=([^&]+)/);
          if(updatedMax){
            var countBeforeUrl = feedBase+labelParam+'?updated-min='+encodeURIComponent(updatedMax[1])+'&max-results=1&alt=json&orderby=updated';
            fetch(countBeforeUrl).then(function(r2){return r2.json();}).then(function(d2){
              var before = parseInt(d2.feed.openSearch$totalResults.$t)||0;
              curPage = Math.ceil(before/MAX_RESULTS);
              if(curPage<1)curPage=1;
              renderPager(totalPages,curPage,newerUrl,olderUrl);
            }).catch(function(){renderPager(totalPages,2,newerUrl,olderUrl);});
            return;
          }
        }
      }
      renderPager(totalPages,curPage,newerUrl,olderUrl);
    })
    .catch(function(){
      // ئەگەر API کار نەکرد، دوگمەی ئاسایی
      renderFallback(newerUrl,olderUrl);
    });

  function renderPager(total,cur,newer,older){
    var pg = document.getElementById('kp-pagination');
    if(!pg)return;
    pg.innerHTML='';
    if(total<=1 && !newer && !older)return;

    // دوگمەی پێشوو (newer)
    if(newer){
      var a=document.createElement('a');
      a.href=newer;a.className='kp-page-btn nav-btn';
      a.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-right"></i>';
      pg.appendChild(a);
    } else {
      var s=document.createElement('span');
      s.className='kp-page-btn nav-btn disabled';
      s.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-right"></i>';
      pg.appendChild(s);
    }

    // ژمارەکان
    var pages = getPageRange(cur,total);
    var prevWasDots = false;
    for(var i=0;i<pages.length;i++){
      var p=pages[i];
      if(p==='...'){
        if(!prevWasDots){var d=document.createElement('span');d.className='kp-page-dots';d.textContent='···';pg.appendChild(d);}
        prevWasDots=true; continue;
      }
      prevWasDots=false;
      if(p===cur){
        var sp=document.createElement('span');sp.className='kp-page-btn active';sp.textContent=p;pg.appendChild(sp);
      } else {
        var url=getPageUrl(p,cur,newer,older,total);
        if(url){var lnk=document.createElement('a');lnk.href=url;lnk.className='kp-page-btn';lnk.textContent=p;pg.appendChild(lnk);}
        else{var sp2=document.createElement('span');sp2.className='kp-page-btn disabled';sp2.textContent=p;pg.appendChild(sp2);}
      }
    }

    // دوگمەی دواتر (older)
    if(older){
      var b=document.createElement('a');
      b.href=older;b.className='kp-page-btn nav-btn';
      b.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-left"></i>';
      pg.appendChild(b);
    } else {
      var s2=document.createElement('span');
      s2.className='kp-page-btn nav-btn disabled';
      s2.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-left"></i>';
      pg.appendChild(s2);
    }
  }

  function getPageRange(cur,total){
    if(total<=7) return Array.from({length:total},function(_,i){return i+1;});
    var r=[1];
    if(cur>3)r.push('...');
    for(var i=Math.max(2,cur-1);i<=Math.min(total-1,cur+1);i++)r.push(i);
    if(cur<total-2)r.push('...');
    r.push(total);
    return r;
  }

  function getPageUrl(p,cur,newer,older,total){
    // پەڕەی یەکەم = homepage
    if(p===1) return window.location.hostname ? 'https://'+window.location.hostname+'/' : '/';
    // پەڕەی کە نزیکی ئێستایە
    if(p===cur-1 && newer) return newer;
    if(p===cur+1 && older) return older;
    // پەڕەی دووری — URL دروست ناکرێت بە Blogger بەبێ token
    return null;
  }

  function renderFallback(newer,older){
    var pg=document.getElementById('kp-pagination');
    if(!pg)return;
    pg.innerHTML='';
    if(newer){var a=document.createElement('a');a.href=newer;a.className='kp-page-btn nav-btn';a.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-right"></i> پێشوو';pg.appendChild(a);}
    if(older){var b=document.createElement('a');b.href=older;b.className='kp-page-btn nav-btn';b.innerHTML='دواتر <i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-left"></i>';pg.appendChild(b);}
  }
})();
//]]>
              </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  //<![CDATA[
  (function(){
    'use strict';
    var dt=document.getElementById('dark-toggle');
    var di=dt?dt.querySelector('i'):null;
    function applyTheme(t){if(t==='dark'){document.body.classList.add('dark');if(di)di.className='fa-solid fa-sun';}else{document.body.classList.remove('dark');if(di)di.className='fa-solid fa-moon';}}
    var st=localStorage.getItem('theme')||(window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches?'dark':'light');
    applyTheme(st);
    if(dt)dt.addEventListener('click',function(){var n=document.body.classList.contains('dark')?'light':'dark';localStorage.setItem('theme',n);applyTheme(n);});
    var pb=document.getElementById('post-body-container');
    var vc=document.getElementById('video-player-container');
    var tb=document.getElementById('tg-overlay-btn');
    var serverBar=document.getElementById('server-bar');

    // ── گلۆبەل: سەرچاوەکان و سێرڤەری ئیستا ──
    window._kpSources={srv1:null,srv2:null};
    window._kpActiveSrv=1; /* بەگشتی srv1 (ڤیدمۆڵ) پێشەوەیە — JS لە خوارەوە دروست دەکات */

    // ══ مێژووی سەیرکردن — دیاریکردنی زوو تا لە هەر شوێنێکی پەڕەدا بەردەست بێت ══
    window.kpAddHistory=function(title,url,thumb){
      try{
        var hist=[];
        var raw=localStorage.getItem('kp_watch_history');
        hist=raw?JSON.parse(raw):[];
        hist=hist.filter(function(it){return it.url!==url;});
        hist.unshift({title:title||'',url:url||'',thumb:thumb||'',watchedAt:new Date().toISOString()});
        if(hist.length>200) hist=hist.slice(0,200);
        localStorage.setItem('kp_watch_history',JSON.stringify(hist));
      }catch(e){}
    };
    // تۆمارکردنی خۆکار کاتێک پەڕەی پۆست کراوەیە
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){
      var _isSingle=!!document.querySelector('.post-title-main');
      if(!_isSingle) return;
      var _title=(document.querySelector('.post-title-main')||{}).textContent||'';
      var _ogImg=document.querySelector('meta[property="og:image"]');
      var _thumb=_ogImg?_ogImg.getAttribute('content'):'';
      window.kpAddHistory(_title.trim(), location.href, _thumb);
    });

    // ── کارخستنی پلەیەر: چاوەڕوانی بارکردنی ناوەڕۆکی پۆست بەبەر MutationObserver ──
    function _kpInitPlayer(){
      var localPb=document.getElementById('post-body-container');
      var localVc=document.getElementById('video-player-container');
      if(!localPb||!localVc) return;

      // ئەگەر پێشتر بارکراوە — دووبارە نەخە (ئایفریم یان srv1 دیاریکراوە)
      if(window._kpSources.srv1||window._kpSources.srv2) return;

      // دەستبەجێی divەکانی زمان لە DOM دەبرێنەوە — تا پلەیەر ئایفریمەکانیان نەبینێت
      ['__kp_orig_body','__kp_body_ar','__kp_body_en','__kp_body_ku'].forEach(function(id){
        var el=localPb.querySelector('#'+id);
        if(el) document.body.appendChild(el);
      });

      var cdnExts=/\.(mp4|webm|m3u8|mkv|ogg|ogv|mov|avi)(\?[^"'\s]*)?$/i;
      var allIframes=localPb.querySelectorAll('iframe');
      var srv1=null,srv2=null;

      allIframes.forEach(function(fr){
        var s=fr.src||'';
        var isYT=/youtube\.com|youtu\.be|youtube-nocookie\.com/.test(s);
        if(isYT&&!srv2) srv2=s;
        else if(!isYT&&!srv1) srv1=s;
      });

      var cdnUrl=null;
      localPb.querySelectorAll('a[href],source[src]').forEach(function(el){
        if(cdnUrl) return;
        var h=el.getAttribute('href')||el.getAttribute('src')||'';
        if(cdnExts.test(h.split('?')[0])) cdnUrl=h;
      });
      if(!cdnUrl){
        var bt=localPb.innerText||localPb.textContent||'';
        var um=bt.match(/https?:\/\/[^\s"'<>]+\.(?:mp4|webm|m3u8|mkv|ogg|ogv|mov)(?:\?[^\s"'<>]*)?/i);
        if(um) cdnUrl=um[0].trim();
      }
      if(cdnUrl&&!srv1) srv1=cdnUrl;

      window._kpSources.srv1=srv1;
      window._kpSources.srv2=srv2;

      var localTb=document.getElementById('tg-overlay-btn');
      var localSB=document.getElementById('server-bar');
      var b1=document.getElementById('srv-btn-1');
      var b2=document.getElementById('srv-btn-2');

      if(srv1){
        /* ڤیدمۆڵ / سێرڤەری یەکەم — ڕاستەوخۆ iframe بارکە، بەبێ poster و بەبێ autoplay=1 */
        if(cdnExts.test((srv1||'').split('?')[0])){
          buildKpPlayer(localVc,srv1);
        }else{
          var fi=makeIframe(srv1);
          localVc.insertBefore(fi,localVc.firstChild);
          kpSetMediaSession();
        }
        if(localTb) localTb.classList.add('visible');
        window._kpActiveSrv=1;
        if(b1)b1.classList.add('active');if(b2)b2.classList.remove('active');
      } else if(srv2){
        /* تەنها YouTube هەیە */
        localVc.insertBefore(makeIframe(srv2),localVc.firstChild);
        kpSetMediaSession();
        if(localTb) localTb.classList.add('visible');
        window._kpActiveSrv=2;
        if(b1)b1.classList.remove('active');if(b2)b2.classList.add('active');
      }

      if(srv1&&srv2&&localSB) localSB.classList.add('visible');

      // ئایفریمەکانی ناوەڕۆک مەخفیبکە (CSSەکە یەکسەر ئەمە کاردەکات)
      allIframes.forEach(function(fr){ fr.style.display='none'; });
    }

    // چاوەڕوانی بارکردنی ناوەڕۆکی پۆست بەبەر MutationObserver
    (function(){
      var inited=false;
      function tryInit(){
        if(inited) return;
        var localPb=document.getElementById('post-body-container');
        if(!localPb||localPb.textContent.trim().length<10) return;
        inited=true;
        _kpInitPlayer();
      }
      // چەند هەوڵی سریع
      tryInit();
      var obs=new MutationObserver(function(){ tryInit(); });
      obs.observe(document.body,{childList:true,subtree:true});
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){ tryInit(); obs.disconnect(); });
      setTimeout(function(){ tryInit(); obs.disconnect(); },3000);
    })();

    // ── Media Session API: دیاریکردنی زانیاری میدیا بۆ lock-screen و notification ──
    function kpSetMediaSession(customTitle,customArtist,customArt){
      if(!('mediaSession' in navigator)) return;
      var t=customTitle||(document.title||'').replace(/\s*\|\s*کوڕی پاک.*/,'').trim()||'کوڕی پاک';
      var a=customArtist||'کوڕی پاک';
      var ogImg=document.querySelector('meta[property="og:image"]');
      var art=customArt||(ogImg?ogImg.getAttribute('content'):'')||'https://i.ibb.co/DPpB0WX6/1000308715.jpg';
      try{
        navigator.mediaSession.metadata=new MediaMetadata({
          title:t,
          artist:a,
          album:'kuripak2026.blogspot.com',
          artwork:[
            {src:art,sizes:'96x96',  type:'image/jpeg'},
            {src:art,sizes:'128x128',type:'image/jpeg'},
            {src:art,sizes:'192x192',type:'image/jpeg'},
            {src:art,sizes:'256x256',type:'image/jpeg'},
            {src:art,sizes:'384x384',type:'image/jpeg'},
            {src:art,sizes:'512x512',type:'image/jpeg'},
            {src:art,sizes:'1200x630',type:'image/jpeg'}
          ]
        });
        // کۆنترۆڵەکان — play/pause بۆ ئایفریم لەڕێی postMessage
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('play',function(){
          var ifrm=document.querySelector('#video-player-container iframe');
          if(ifrm){try{ifrm.contentWindow.postMessage('{"method":"play"}','*');}catch(e){}}
        });
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('pause',function(){
          var ifrm=document.querySelector('#video-player-container iframe');
          if(ifrm){try{ifrm.contentWindow.postMessage('{"method":"pause"}','*');}catch(e){}}
        });
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('seekbackward',function(d){
          var ifrm=document.querySelector('#video-player-container iframe');
          var s=d&&d.seekOffset?d.seekOffset:10;
          if(ifrm){try{ifrm.contentWindow.postMessage(JSON.stringify({method:'seekBy',value:-s}),'*');}catch(e){}}
        });
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('seekforward',function(d){
          var ifrm=document.querySelector('#video-player-container iframe');
          var s=d&&d.seekOffset?d.seekOffset:10;
          if(ifrm){try{ifrm.contentWindow.postMessage(JSON.stringify({method:'seekBy',value:s}),'*');}catch(e){}}
        });
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('stop',function(){
          var ifrm=document.querySelector('#video-player-container iframe');
          if(ifrm){try{ifrm.contentWindow.postMessage('{"method":"pause"}','*');}catch(e){}}
        });
        // nexttrack/previoustrack — تەنها ئەگەر هەبوو
        try{navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('nexttrack',null);}catch(e){}
        try{navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('previoustrack',null);}catch(e){}
      }catch(e){}
    }
    window.kpSetMediaSession=kpSetMediaSession;

    // ── یارمەتیدەری iframe درووستکردن ──
    function makeIframe(src){
      var f=document.createElement('iframe');
      f.src=src;
      f.setAttribute('allowfullscreen','');
      f.setAttribute('frameborder','0');
      /* allow ی تەواو: ئۆتۆپلە + فولسکرین + PiP پێویستن بۆ ڤیدمۆڵ، Safari و Firefox */
      f.setAttribute('allow','accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share; fullscreen');
      f.style.cssText='position:absolute;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;border:0';

      return f;
    }

    // ── پۆستەر / Lazy iframe بۆ ڤیدمۆڵ و سێرڤەرە ئایفریمییەکان ──
    function makePoster(src){
      var ogImg=document.querySelector('meta[property="og:image"]');
      var posterSrc=ogImg?ogImg.getAttribute('content'):'';
      var wrap=document.createElement('div');
      wrap.style.cssText='position:absolute;inset:0;background:#111;cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;overflow:hidden;';
      if(posterSrc&&posterSrc.indexOf('kuri-pak-logo')===-1){
        var img=document.createElement('img');
        img.src=posterSrc;img.alt='';
        img.style.cssText='position:absolute;inset:0;width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;filter:brightness(.65);transition:filter .3s;';
        wrap.appendChild(img);
        wrap.addEventListener('mouseenter',function(){img.style.filter='brightness(.8)';});
        wrap.addEventListener('mouseleave',function(){img.style.filter='brightness(.65)';});
      }
      var btn=document.createElement('div');
      btn.style.cssText='position:relative;z-index:2;width:72px;height:72px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.95);border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;box-shadow:0 4px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.55);transition:transform .2s,box-shadow .2s;';
      btn.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid fa-play" style="color:var(--primary,#1b6b5e);font-size:27px;margin-left:6px;"></i>';
      wrap.appendChild(btn);
      wrap.addEventListener('mouseenter',function(){btn.style.transform='scale(1.12)';btn.style.boxShadow='0 6px 32px rgba(0,0,0,.65)';});
      wrap.addEventListener('mouseleave',function(){btn.style.transform='';btn.style.boxShadow='0 4px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.55)';});
      wrap.addEventListener('click',function(){
        wrap.remove();
        var f=makeIframe(src);
        var sep=src.indexOf('?')>=0?'&':'?';
        f.src=src+sep+'autoplay=1';
        vc.insertBefore(f,vc.firstChild);
        kpSetMediaSession();
      });
      return wrap;
    }

    // ── نیشاندانی سێرڤەری دیاریکراو ──
    window.kpSwitchServer=function(n){
      var src=window._kpSources['srv'+n];
      if(!src||n===window._kpActiveSrv) return;
      window._kpActiveSrv=n;
      // دوگمەکان نوێبکەوە
      document.querySelectorAll('.srv-btn').forEach(function(b){
        b.classList.toggle('active',parseInt(b.dataset.srv)===n);
      });
      // پلەیەرەکە پاکبکەوە
      var cdnExts=/\.(mp4|webm|m3u8|mkv|ogg|ogv|mov|avi)/i;
      vc.querySelectorAll('.kp-wrap,iframe').forEach(function(el){el.remove();});
      if(cdnExts.test(src)){
        buildKpPlayer(vc,src);
      }else{
        vc.insertBefore(makeIframe(src),vc.firstChild);
        kpSetMediaSession();
      }
      if(tb) tb.classList.add('visible');
    };

    // ══ ڤیدیۆی دواتر: دەرخستنی ئۆڤەرلەی کاتێک ڤیدیۆ تەواو دەبێت ══
    window.kpTriggerNextVideo = function(){
      var localVc = document.getElementById('video-player-container');
      if(!localVc) return;
      // ئەگەر پێشتر ئۆڤەرلەی هەیە، دووبارە نەخە
      if(localVc.querySelector('.kp-next-overlay')) return;

      var labelEl = document.getElementById('kp-post-label-el');
      var urlEl   = document.getElementById('kp-post-url-el');
      var label   = labelEl ? labelEl.textContent.trim() : '';
      var curUrl  = urlEl   ? urlEl.textContent.trim()  : location.href;

      if(!label) return; // لەیبڵ نییە، هیچ مەکە

      // فێچی JSON API بۆ هەمان لەیبڵ
      var apiUrl = location.origin + '/feeds/posts/default/-/' +
                   encodeURIComponent(label) + '?max-results=10&alt=json&orderby=published';
      fetch(apiUrl)
        .then(function(r){ return r.json(); })
        .then(function(d){
          var entries = (d.feed && d.feed.entry) || [];
          // پۆستی دواتر بدۆزەوە — ئەوەی ناونیشانەکەی جیاوازە لە ئیستا
          var next = null;
          for(var i=0; i<entries.length; i++){
            var e = entries[i];
            var eUrl = '';
            (e.link||[]).forEach(function(l){ if(l.rel==='alternate') eUrl=l.href; });
            // پۆستی ئیستا دیار بکە و بازبدە
            if(eUrl && eUrl.replace(/\/$/,'') !== curUrl.replace(/\/$/,'')){
              next = {
                url:   eUrl,
                title: (e.title && e.title.$t) || '',
                thumb: e['media$thumbnail']
                        ? e['media$thumbnail'].url.replace(/\/s[0-9]+-c\//,'/s320-c/')
                        : (function(){ var m=(e.content&&e.content.$t||'').match(/youtube\.com\/vi\/([^\/]+)\//);
                                       return m ? 'https://i.ytimg.com/vi/'+m[1]+'/mqdefault.jpg' : ''; })()
              };
              break;
            }
          }
          if(!next) return; // پۆستی دواتر نەدۆزرایەوە

          // ══ ئۆڤەرلەی بنێ ══
          var ov = document.createElement('div');
          ov.className = 'kp-next-overlay';

          // ژمارەی کاوتداون
          var COUNTDOWN = 7;
          var remaining = COUNTDOWN;
          var timer = null;
          var CIRC = 2 * Math.PI * 22; // r=22 → 138.2

          ov.innerHTML =
            '<div class="kp-next-label">ڤیدیۆی دواتر لە هەمان پۆل</div>' +
            '<a class="kp-next-card" href="'+next.url+'" id="kp-next-card-link">' +
              (next.thumb
                ? '<img class="kp-next-thumb" src="'+next.thumb+'" alt="" loading="lazy" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">'
                : '<div class="kp-next-thumb" style="background:#222;border-radius:6px"></div>') +
              '<div class="kp-next-info">' +
                '<div class="kp-next-title">'+next.title+'</div>' +
                '<div class="kp-next-sub"><i class="fa-solid fa-tag" style="font-size:9px;margin-left:3px"></i>'+label+'</div>' +
              '</div>' +
              '<div class="kp-next-countdown-ring">' +
                '<svg width="52" height="52" viewBox="0 0 52 52">' +
                  '<circle cx="26" cy="26" r="22"/>' +
                  '<circle class="kp-nring-fill" id="kp-ring-fill" cx="26" cy="26" r="22" stroke-dasharray="'+CIRC+'" stroke-dashoffset="0"/>' +
                '</svg>' +
                '<div class="kp-next-countdown-num" id="kp-countdown-num">'+COUNTDOWN+'</div>' +
              '</div>' +
            '</a>' +
            '<div class="kp-next-actions">' +
              '<button class="kp-next-play-now" id="kp-next-now-btn"><i class="fa-solid fa-play" style="margin-left:5px"></i>ئێستا بڕۆ</button>' +
              '<button class="kp-next-cancel" id="kp-next-cancel-btn"><i class="fa-solid fa-xmark" style="margin-left:4px"></i>هەڵوەشاندنەوە</button>' +
            '</div>';

          localVc.appendChild(ov);

          var ringFill = document.getElementById('kp-ring-fill');
          var numEl    = document.getElementById('kp-countdown-num');

          function tick(){
            remaining--;
            if(numEl) numEl.textContent = remaining;
            if(ringFill) ringFill.style.strokeDashoffset = (CIRC * (1 - remaining/COUNTDOWN)).toFixed(2);
            if(remaining <= 0){
              clearInterval(timer);
              location.href = next.url;
            }
          }
          timer = setInterval(tick, 1000);
          // ئیستا بڕۆ
          var nowBtn = document.getElementById('kp-next-now-btn');
          if(nowBtn) nowBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e){
            e.preventDefault();
            clearInterval(timer);
            location.href = next.url;
          });
          // هەڵوەشاندنەوە
          var cancelBtn = document.getElementById('kp-next-cancel-btn');
          if(cancelBtn) cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
            clearInterval(timer);
            ov.remove();
          });
        })
        .catch(function(){}); // بێدەنگ شکستبهێنا
    };

    // ══ پلەیلیستی پۆل — زنجیرەیی بەشێوەی Natural Sort ══
    (function(){
      var labelEl=document.getElementById('kp-post-label-el');
      var urlEl=document.getElementById('kp-post-url-el');
      var plistSection=document.getElementById('kp-playlist-section');
      var plistEl=document.getElementById('kp-playlist-list');
      var chipEl=document.getElementById('kp-playlist-label-chip');
      var autoChk=document.getElementById('kp-autoplay-chk');
      if(!labelEl||!plistSection||!plistEl) return;

      var label=labelEl.textContent.trim();
      var curUrl=(urlEl?urlEl.textContent.trim():location.href).replace(/\/$/,'');
      if(!label) return;

      // ── پاشەکەوتی toggle ──
      try{if(localStorage.getItem('kp_autoplay_pl')==='1') autoChk.checked=true;}catch(e){}
      if(autoChk) autoChk.addEventListener('change',function(){
        try{localStorage.setItem('kp_autoplay_pl',this.checked?'1':'0');}catch(e){}
      });

      if(chipEl) chipEl.textContent=label;

      // Natural sort بۆ ڤیدیۆکان
      function natSort(a,b){
        var ra=(a||'').replace(/[٠-٩]/g,function(d){return d.charCodeAt(0)-1632;}).replace(/[۰-۹]/g,function(d){return d.charCodeAt(0)-1776;});
        var rb=(b||'').replace(/[٠-٩]/g,function(d){return d.charCodeAt(0)-1632;}).replace(/[۰-۹]/g,function(d){return d.charCodeAt(0)-1776;});
        var re=/(\d+)|(\D+)/g; var ta=ra.match(re)||[]; var tb=rb.match(re)||[];
        for(var i=0;i<Math.max(ta.length,tb.length);i++){
          if(i>=ta.length)return -1; if(i>=tb.length)return 1;
          var na=parseInt(ta[i],10),nb=parseInt(tb[i],10);
          if(!isNaN(na)&&!isNaN(nb)){if(na!==nb)return na-nb;}
          else{var c=ta[i].localeCompare(tb[i],'ku');if(c!==0)return c;}
        }
        return 0;
      }

      fetch(location.origin+'/feeds/posts/default/-/'+encodeURIComponent(label)+'?max-results=50&alt=json&orderby=published')
        .then(function(r){return r.json();})
        .then(function(d){
          var entries=(d.feed&&d.feed.entry)||[];
          if(entries.length<2){ plistSection.style.display='none'; return; }

          var posts=entries.map(function(e){
            var eUrl=''; (e.link||[]).forEach(function(l){if(l.rel==='alternate')eUrl=l.href;});
            var thumb='';
            if(e['media$thumbnail']) thumb=e['media$thumbnail'].url.replace(/\/s[0-9]+-c\//,'/s320-c/');
            else{var m=(e.content&&e.content.$t||'').match(/youtube\.com\/vi\/([^\/]+)\//);if(m)thumb='https://i.ytimg.com/vi/'+m[1]+'/mqdefault.jpg';}
            var pubDate=e.published&&e.published.$t?new Date(e.published.$t):new Date(0);
            return {title:(e.title&&e.title.$t)||'',url:eUrl,thumb:thumb,pub:pubDate};
          });

          // ڕیزبەندی بەپێی بەرواری بارکردن — کۆنترین (بەشی ١) لەسەرەوە
          posts.sort(function(a,b){return a.pub-b.pub;});

          var curIdx=0;
          posts.forEach(function(p,i){if(p.url.replace(/\/$/,'')=== curUrl) curIdx=i;});

          plistSection.style.display='';

          plistEl.innerHTML=posts.map(function(p,i){
            var isCur=p.url.replace(/\/$/,'')=== curUrl;
            var imgH=p.thumb?'<img class="kp-playlist-thumb" src="'+p.thumb+'" alt="" loading="lazy" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">'
                            :'<div class="kp-playlist-thumb" style="background:var(--bg-hover)"></div>';
            return '<a class="kp-playlist-item'+(isCur?' active':'')+'" href="'+p.url+'" onclick="kpPlaylistClick(event,this)">'
              +'<span class="kp-playlist-num">'+(isCur?'<i class="fa-solid fa-play" style="font-size:8px"></i>':(i+1))+'</span>'
              +imgH
              +'<div class="kp-playlist-info">'
                +'<div class="kp-playlist-name">'+p.title+'</div>'
                +'<div class="kp-playlist-playing">ئێستا پخشدەبێت</div>'
              +'</div>'
              +'</a>';
          }).join('');

          // ── scroll بۆ بابەتی ئیستا ──
          var activeItem=plistEl.querySelector('.kp-playlist-item.active');
          if(activeItem) setTimeout(function(){activeItem.scrollIntoView({block:'nearest',behavior:'smooth'});},400);

          // ── Auto-play nexttrack: پاشخانی کاتی کۆتایی ڤیدیۆ ──
          window._kpPlaylistPosts=posts;
          window._kpPlaylistCurIdx=curIdx;
        })
        .catch(function(){});
    })();

    window.kpPlaylistClick=function(e,el){
      var href=el.getAttribute('href');
      if(!href) return;
      var chk=document.getElementById('kp-autoplay-chk');
      // ئەگەر ئەو بابەتەیە کە ئێستاشە، بڕۆ
      if(el.classList.contains('active')){ e.preventDefault(); return; }
      // ئاسایی: ئیجازەی navigator
    };

    // ── Auto-play دوای کۆتایی ڤیدیۆ ──
    var _origNext=window.kpTriggerNextVideo;
    window.kpTriggerNextVideo=function(){
      var chk=document.getElementById('kp-autoplay-chk');
      if(chk&&chk.checked&&window._kpPlaylistPosts){
        var nextIdx=window._kpPlaylistCurIdx+1;
        if(nextIdx<window._kpPlaylistPosts.length){
          location.href=window._kpPlaylistPosts[nextIdx].url;
          return;
        }
      }
      if(_origNext) _origNext();
    };

    // ══ پلەیلیستی پۆل — کۆتا ══
    function buildKpPlayer(container,src){
      // DOM
      var wrap=document.createElement('div');wrap.className='kp-wrap buffering';
      var vid=document.createElement('video');
      vid.preload='metadata';vid.playsInline=true;
      // ── HLS.js: بۆ لینکی .m3u8 ── با Quality Selector
      var _hlsInst=null;
      (function(){
        var isHls=/\.m3u8/i.test(src);
        if(isHls){
          if(typeof Hls!=='undefined'&&Hls.isSupported()){
            _hlsInst=new Hls({capLevelToPlayerSize:true});
            _hlsInst.loadSource(src);_hlsInst.attachMedia(vid);
          }else if(vid.canPlayType('application/vnd.apple.mpegurl')){
            vid.src=src;
          }else{
            vid.src=src;
          }
        }else{
          vid.src=src;
        }
      })();
      vid.style.cssText='width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:contain;display:block';
      var grad=document.createElement('div');grad.className='kp-gradient';
      var spin=document.createElement('div');spin.className='kp-spinner';
      var flash=document.createElement('div');flash.className='kp-flash';
      var ctrls=document.createElement('div');ctrls.className='kp-controls';
      // پڕۆگرێس
      var prog=document.createElement('div');prog.className='kp-prog';
      var track=document.createElement('div');track.className='kp-prog-track';
      var pbuf=document.createElement('div');pbuf.className='kp-prog-buf';
      var pfill=document.createElement('div');pfill.className='kp-prog-fill';pfill.style.width='0%';
      var pthumb=document.createElement('div');pthumb.className='kp-prog-thumb';
      var tip=document.createElement('div');tip.className='kp-tooltip';tip.style.left='0px';
      track.appendChild(pbuf);track.appendChild(pfill);track.appendChild(pthumb);
      prog.appendChild(track);prog.appendChild(tip);
      // ڕیز
      var row=document.createElement('div');row.className='kp-row';
      function btn(ic,lbl){var b=document.createElement('button');b.className='kp-btn';b.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid '+ic+'"></i>';b.title=lbl;return b;}
      var bPlay=btn('fa-play','لێدان / وەستان');
      var bRew=btn('fa-rotate-left','١٠ چرکە بۆ دواوە');bRew.style.fontSize='15px';
      var bFwd=btn('fa-rotate-right','١٠ چرکە بۆ پێشەوە');bFwd.style.fontSize='15px';
      // دەنگ
      var vg=document.createElement('div');vg.className='kp-vol-group';
      var bVol=btn('fa-volume-high','دەنگ');
      var vSlide=document.createElement('input');
      vSlide.type='range';vSlide.className='kp-vol-slider';
      vSlide.min=0;vSlide.max=1;vSlide.step=0.02;vSlide.value=1;
      vg.appendChild(bVol);vg.appendChild(vSlide);
      var timeEl=document.createElement('span');timeEl.className='kp-time';timeEl.textContent='0:00 / 0:00';
      var sp=document.createElement('div');sp.className='kp-spacer';
      // ── پاشەکەوتکردنی خێرایی (Speed Memory) ──
      var _savedSpeed=1;
      try{var _ss=parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('kp_speed'));if(_ss&&speeds.indexOf(_ss)>=0){_savedSpeed=_ss;spIdx=speeds.indexOf(_ss);}}catch(e){}
      var bSpeed=document.createElement('button');bSpeed.className='kp-speed';bSpeed.textContent=_savedSpeed+'×';bSpeed.title='خێرایی';
      vid.playbackRate=_savedSpeed;
      // ── دوگمەی PiP ──
      var bPip=btn('fa-clone','وێنە-لەناو-وێنە (PiP)');bPip.style.fontSize='14px';
      // ── دوگمەی فولسکرین ──
      var bFs=btn('fa-expand','پڕشاشە');
      // ── دوگمەی کوالێتی (Quality) ──
      var bQuality=document.createElement('button');bQuality.className='kp-btn kp-quality-btn';bQuality.title='کوالێتی';bQuality.textContent='خودکار';
      bQuality.style.fontSize='11px';bQuality.style.fontWeight='700';bQuality.style.minWidth='42px';
      // ── دوگمەی ژێرنووس (Subtitle) ──
      var bSub=btn('fa-closed-captioning','ژێرنووس');bSub.style.fontSize='14px';
      var _subTrack=null;var _subVisible=false;
      // ── مێنوی کوالێتی ──
      var qualMenu=document.createElement('div');qualMenu.className='kp-quality-menu';qualMenu.style.cssText='display:none;position:absolute;bottom:52px;left:8px;background:rgba(20,20,20,.95);border-radius:10px;padding:6px;min-width:110px;z-index:20;box-shadow:0 4px 16px rgba(0,0,0,.6)';
      wrap.appendChild(qualMenu);
      function buildQualityMenu(){
        if(!_hlsInst||!_hlsInst.levels||_hlsInst.levels.length<2){bQuality.style.display='none';return;}
        bQuality.style.display='';
        qualMenu.innerHTML='';
        var autoBtn=document.createElement('button');
        autoBtn.textContent='خودکار';autoBtn.style.cssText='display:block;width:100%;padding:7px 12px;background:none;border:none;color:#fff;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer;border-radius:6px;text-align:right;font-family:inherit';
        autoBtn.onmouseenter=function(){this.style.background='rgba(255,255,255,.12)';};autoBtn.onmouseleave=function(){this.style.background='none';};
        autoBtn.onclick=function(){_hlsInst.currentLevel=-1;bQuality.textContent='خودکار';qualMenu.style.display='none';};
        qualMenu.appendChild(autoBtn);
        _hlsInst.levels.forEach(function(lv,i){
          var label=(lv.height?lv.height+'p':'ئاستی '+(i+1));
          var lb=document.createElement('button');
          lb.textContent=label;lb.style.cssText='display:block;width:100%;padding:7px 12px;background:none;border:none;color:#ccc;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer;border-radius:6px;text-align:right;font-family:inherit';
          lb.onmouseenter=function(){this.style.background='rgba(255,255,255,.12)';};lb.onmouseleave=function(){this.style.background='none';};
          lb.onclick=function(){_hlsInst.currentLevel=i;bQuality.textContent=label;qualMenu.style.display='none';};
          qualMenu.appendChild(lb);
        });
      }
      if(_hlsInst){
        _hlsInst.on(Hls.Events.MANIFEST_PARSED,function(){buildQualityMenu();});
      } else {
        bQuality.style.display='none';
      }
      bQuality.onclick=function(e){
        e.stopPropagation();
        qualMenu.style.display=qualMenu.style.display==='none'?'block':'none';
      };
      // ── ژێرنووس ──
      bSub.onclick=function(){
        var ti=vid.textTracks[0];
        if(!ti){kpToast('فایلی ژێرنووس نییە',true);return;}
        _subVisible=!_subVisible;
        ti.mode=_subVisible?'showing':'disabled';
        bSub.style.color=_subVisible?'var(--primary)':'';
        kpToast(_subVisible?'ژێرنووس کراوەتەوە':'ژێرنووس داخراوە');
      };
      // ── پاشەکەوتکردنی فایلی ژێرنووس دەرەکی ──
      (function(){
        /* ئەگەر لە post-body دا <track> یان data-sub-url هەبوو */
        var subUrl=container.dataset&&container.dataset.subUrl;
        if(!subUrl){
          var tm=document.querySelector('[data-sub-url]');
          if(tm) subUrl=tm.dataset.subUrl;
        }
        if(subUrl){
          var tr=document.createElement('track');
          tr.kind='subtitles';tr.src=subUrl;tr.default=false;
          vid.appendChild(tr);
        }
      })();
      row.appendChild(bPlay);row.appendChild(bRew);row.appendChild(bFwd);
      row.appendChild(vg);row.appendChild(timeEl);row.appendChild(sp);row.appendChild(bSpeed);row.appendChild(bQuality);row.appendChild(bSub);row.appendChild(bPip);row.appendChild(bFs);
      ctrls.appendChild(prog);ctrls.appendChild(row);
      wrap.appendChild(vid);wrap.appendChild(grad);wrap.appendChild(spin);wrap.appendChild(flash);wrap.appendChild(ctrls);
      container.appendChild(wrap);
      // hide quality menu on outside click
      document.addEventListener('click',function(e){if(!wrap.contains(e.target))qualMenu.style.display='none';});

      // ── یارمەتیدەر ──
      var hideTimer=null;
      var speeds=[0.25,0.5,0.75,1,1.25,1.5,1.75,2];

      function fmt(s){
        s=Math.floor(s||0);
        var h=Math.floor(s/3600),m=Math.floor((s%3600)/60),sec=s%60;
        if(h>0) return h+':'+(m<10?'0':'')+m+':'+(sec<10?'0':'')+sec;
        return m+':'+(sec<10?'0':'')+sec;
      }

      function showUI(){
        wrap.classList.add('ui-visible');
        wrap.style.cursor='default';
        clearTimeout(hideTimer);
        if(!vid.paused) hideTimer=setTimeout(hideUI,3000);
      }
      function hideUI(){
        if(vid.paused) return;
        wrap.classList.remove('ui-visible');
        wrap.style.cursor='none';
      }

      function doFlash(ic){
        flash.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid '+ic+'"></i>';
        flash.classList.remove('pop');
        void flash.offsetWidth;
        flash.classList.add('pop');
      }

      function setVol(){
        var v=vid.muted?0:vid.volume;
        var ic=v===0?'fa-volume-xmark':v<0.5?'fa-volume-low':'fa-volume-high';
        bVol.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid '+ic+'"></i>';
        vSlide.value=v;
        // رەنگی slider
        vSlide.style.background='linear-gradient(to right,#fff '+Math.round(v*100)+'%,rgba(255,255,255,.3) '+Math.round(v*100)+'%)';
      }

      function updateProgress(){
        var c=vid.currentTime,du=vid.duration||0;
        var pct=du>0?(c/du)*100:0;
        pfill.style.width=pct+'%';
        pthumb.style.left=pct+'%';
        if(vid.buffered.length>0){
          var bp=du>0?(vid.buffered.end(vid.buffered.length-1)/du)*100:0;
          pbuf.style.width=bp+'%';
        }
        timeEl.textContent=fmt(c)+' / '+fmt(du);
      }

      function setPlay(playing){
        wrap.classList.toggle('playing',playing);
        bPlay.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid '+(playing?'fa-pause':'fa-play')+'"></i>';
      }

      function togglePlay(){
        if(vid.paused){vid.play();}else{vid.pause();}
      }

      // ── ئیڤێنتەکانی ڤیدیۆ ──
      vid.addEventListener('loadedmetadata',function(){
        updateProgress();wrap.classList.remove('buffering');
        // ── دەستپێکردنەوە لەو خولەکەی وەستابوو (Resume Playback) ──
        try{
          var _rKey='kp_resume_'+btoa(encodeURIComponent(src||location.pathname)).slice(0,40);
          var _rt=parseFloat(localStorage.getItem(_rKey));
          if(_rt&&_rt>5&&vid.duration&&_rt<vid.duration-5){
            vid.currentTime=_rt;
          }
        }catch(e){}
      });
      vid.addEventListener('waiting',function(){wrap.classList.add('buffering');});
      vid.addEventListener('canplay',function(){wrap.classList.remove('buffering');});
      vid.addEventListener('playing',function(){wrap.classList.remove('buffering');setPlay(true);showUI();
        // ── Media Session بۆ Native Player ──
        kpSetMediaSession();
        if('mediaSession' in navigator){
          try{
            navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('play',  function(){vid.play();});
            navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('pause', function(){vid.pause();});
            navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('seekbackward',function(d){vid.currentTime=Math.max(0,vid.currentTime-(d&&d.seekOffset?d.seekOffset:10));});
            navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('seekforward', function(d){vid.currentTime=Math.min(vid.duration||0,vid.currentTime+(d&&d.seekOffset?d.seekOffset:10));});
            navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('stop',  function(){vid.pause();vid.currentTime=0;});
          }catch(e){}
        }
      });
      vid.addEventListener('pause',function(){setPlay(false);showUI();});
      vid.addEventListener('ended',function(){setPlay(false);showUI();kpTriggerNextVideo();});
      vid.addEventListener('timeupdate',function(){
        updateProgress();
        // ── پاشەکەوتکردنی خولەک (Resume Save) ──
        try{
          var _rKey='kp_resume_'+btoa(encodeURIComponent(src||location.pathname)).slice(0,40);
          if(vid.currentTime>5) localStorage.setItem(_rKey,vid.currentTime.toFixed(1));
        }catch(e){}
        if('mediaSession' in navigator&&vid.duration&&!isNaN(vid.duration)){
          try{navigator.mediaSession.setPositionState({duration:vid.duration,playbackRate:vid.playbackRate||1,position:vid.currentTime});}catch(e){}
        }
      });
      vid.addEventListener('volumechange',setVol);
      vid.addEventListener('error',function(){
        wrap.innerHTML='<div style="position:absolute;inset:0;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;color:#fff;gap:10px"><i class="fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation" style="font-size:36px;opacity:.5"></i><span style="font-size:14px;opacity:.7">ڤیدیۆکە بار نەکرا</span></div>';
      });

      // ── کلیک لەسەر ڤیدیۆ ──
      var clickTimer=null;
      wrap.addEventListener('click',function(e){
        if(e.target.closest('.kp-controls')) return;
        clearTimeout(clickTimer);
        clickTimer=setTimeout(function(){togglePlay();doFlash(vid.paused?'fa-pause':'fa-play');},200);
      });
      // دەبڵ کلیک: فولسکرین
      wrap.addEventListener('dblclick',function(e){
        if(e.target.closest('.kp-controls')) return;
        clearTimeout(clickTimer);
        toggleFs();
      });

      // ── موس موڤ: نیشاندانی UI ──
      wrap.addEventListener('mousemove',showUI);
      wrap.addEventListener('mouseenter',showUI);
      wrap.addEventListener('mouseleave',function(){if(!vid.paused) hideUI();});

      // ── دوگمەکان ──
      bPlay.addEventListener('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();togglePlay();});
      bRew.addEventListener('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();vid.currentTime=Math.max(0,vid.currentTime-10);doFlash('fa-rotate-left');showUI();});
      bFwd.addEventListener('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();vid.currentTime=Math.min(vid.duration||0,vid.currentTime+10);doFlash('fa-rotate-right');showUI();});

      // ── دەنگ ──
      bVol.addEventListener('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();vid.muted=!vid.muted;});
      vSlide.addEventListener('input',function(e){e.stopPropagation();vid.volume=parseFloat(this.value);vid.muted=vid.volume===0;});
      vSlide.addEventListener('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();});

      // ── خێرایی + Speed Memory ──
      bSpeed.addEventListener('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();spIdx=(spIdx+1)%speeds.length;vid.playbackRate=speeds[spIdx];this.textContent=speeds[spIdx]+'×';try{localStorage.setItem('kp_speed',speeds[spIdx]);}catch(ex){}showUI();});

      // ── PiP (Picture-in-Picture) ──
      bPip.addEventListener('click',function(e){
        e.stopPropagation();
        if(document.pictureInPictureElement){
          document.exitPictureInPicture().catch(function(){});
        }else if(document.pictureInPictureEnabled){
          vid.requestPictureInPicture().catch(function(){});
        }
      });
      vid.addEventListener('enterpictureinpicture',function(){ bPip.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid fa-compress-alt"></i>'; });
      vid.addEventListener('leavepictureinpicture',function(){ bPip.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid fa-clone"></i>'; });
      // PiP نەیبیت، شاردنەوەی دوگمە
      if(!document.pictureInPictureEnabled) bPip.style.display='none';

      // ── فولسکرین ──
      function toggleFs(){
        var el=wrap.parentElement;
        if(!document.fullscreenElement){
          (el.requestFullscreen||el.webkitRequestFullscreen||el.mozRequestFullScreen||function(){}).call(el);
        }else{
          (document.exitFullscreen||document.webkitExitFullscreen||document.mozCancelFullScreen||function(){}).call(document);
        }
      }
      bFs.addEventListener('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();toggleFs();});
      document.addEventListener('fullscreenchange',function(){
        bFs.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid '+(document.fullscreenElement?'fa-compress':'fa-expand')+'"></i>';
      });

      // ── پڕۆگرێس بار ──
      var seeking=false;
      function pctFromEvent(e){
        var r=track.getBoundingClientRect();
        var clientX=e.touches?e.touches[0].clientX:e.clientX;
        return Math.max(0,Math.min(1,(clientX-r.left)/r.width));
      }
      function applySeek(pct){
        if(vid.duration) vid.currentTime=pct*vid.duration;
        pfill.style.width=(pct*100)+'%';
        pthumb.style.left=(pct*100)+'%';
      }
      prog.addEventListener('mousedown',function(e){
        e.preventDefault();e.stopPropagation();
        seeking=true;applySeek(pctFromEvent(e));showUI();
      });
      window.addEventListener('mousemove',function(e){if(seeking){applySeek(pctFromEvent(e));}});
      window.addEventListener('mouseup',function(){seeking=false;});
      // tooltip لەسەر ماوس موڤ لە پڕۆگرێس
      prog.addEventListener('mousemove',function(e){
        var r=track.getBoundingClientRect();
        var pct=Math.max(0,Math.min(1,(e.clientX-r.left)/r.width));
        tip.textContent=fmt((vid.duration||0)*pct);
        tip.style.left=(pct*100)+'%';
      });
      // تاچ
      prog.addEventListener('touchstart',function(e){e.preventDefault();seeking=true;applySeek(pctFromEvent(e));},{passive:false});
      prog.addEventListener('touchmove',function(e){e.preventDefault();if(seeking)applySeek(pctFromEvent(e));},{passive:false});
      prog.addEventListener('touchend',function(){seeking=false;});

      // ── کیبۆرد ──
      document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){
        if(document.activeElement&&['INPUT','TEXTAREA','SELECT'].indexOf(document.activeElement.tagName)>=0) return;
        if(!document.contains(wrap)) return;
        if(e.code==='Space'||e.key===' '){e.preventDefault();togglePlay();doFlash(vid.paused?'fa-pause':'fa-play');showUI();}
        else if(e.code==='ArrowRight'){e.preventDefault();vid.currentTime=Math.min(vid.duration||0,vid.currentTime+10);doFlash('fa-forward-fast');showUI();}
        else if(e.code==='ArrowLeft'){e.preventDefault();vid.currentTime=Math.max(0,vid.currentTime-10);doFlash('fa-backward-fast');showUI();}
        else if(e.code==='ArrowUp'){e.preventDefault();vid.volume=Math.min(1,vid.volume+0.1);showUI();}
        else if(e.code==='ArrowDown'){e.preventDefault();vid.volume=Math.max(0,vid.volume-0.1);showUI();}
        else if(e.code==='KeyM'){vid.muted=!vid.muted;showUI();}
        else if(e.code==='KeyF'){toggleFs();}
      });

      // ── تاچ: دەبڵ-تاچ چەپ/ڕاست ──
      var lastTap=0;var tapTimer=null;
      wrap.addEventListener('touchend',function(e){
        if(e.target.closest('.kp-controls,.kp-prog')) return;
        var now=Date.now();
        if(now-lastTap<280){
          clearTimeout(tapTimer);
          var r=wrap.getBoundingClientRect();
          var x=e.changedTouches[0].clientX-r.left;
          if(x<r.width*0.35){vid.currentTime=Math.max(0,vid.currentTime-10);doFlash('fa-backward-fast');}
          else if(x>r.width*0.65){vid.currentTime=Math.min(vid.duration||0,vid.currentTime+10);doFlash('fa-forward-fast');}
          else{toggleFs();}
        }else{
          tapTimer=setTimeout(function(){togglePlay();showUI();},280);
        }
        lastTap=now;
      });

      // start
      showUI();
      setVol();
    }
    var sl=document.getElementById('site-header');
    var os=document.getElementById('open-search');
    var cs=document.getElementById('close-search');
    var si=document.getElementById('search-input');
    var kpSuggestBox=document.getElementById('kp-suggestions');
    var _suggestTimer=null,_suggestCache={};

    function openSearch(){
      if(!sl) return;
      sl.classList.add('search-active');
      if(si) setTimeout(function(){si.focus();},180);
    }
    function closeSearch(){
      if(!sl) return;
      sl.classList.remove('search-active');
      if(kpSuggestBox) kpSuggestBox.classList.remove('open');
    }
    if(os) os.addEventListener('click',openSearch);
    if(cs) cs.addEventListener('click',closeSearch);
    document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){if(e.key==='Escape') closeSearch();});

    // ── گەڕانی زیندوو (نوێکراوە: Highlighting + Keyboard Nav + Search History) ──
    var _KP_HIST_KEY='kp_search_hist';
    var _kbdIdx=-1;

    function _kpGetHistory(){
      try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(_KP_HIST_KEY)||'[]');}catch(e){return[];}
    }
    function _kpSaveHistory(q){
      var h=_kpGetHistory().filter(function(x){return x!==q;});
      h.unshift(q);
      try{localStorage.setItem(_KP_HIST_KEY,JSON.stringify(h.slice(0,5)));}catch(e){}
    }
    function _kpClearHistory(){
      try{localStorage.removeItem(_KP_HIST_KEY);}catch(e){}
      if(kpSuggestBox) kpSuggestBox.classList.remove('open');
    }

    function _kpHighlight(text,q){
      if(!q) return text;
      try{
        var re=new RegExp('('+q.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g,'\\$&')+')','gi');
        return text.replace(re,'<mark class="kp-sugg-highlight">$1</mark>');
      }catch(e){return text;}
    }

    function _kpShowSug(posts,q){
      if(!kpSuggestBox) return;
      _kbdIdx=-1;
      if(!posts||!posts.length){
        kpSuggestBox.innerHTML='<div class="kp-sugg-empty">هیچ بابەتێک نەدۆزرایەوە</div>';
        kpSuggestBox.classList.add('open');return;
      }
      var h='';
      posts.slice(0,7).forEach(function(p){
        var titleHL=_kpHighlight(p.title,q);
        h+='<a class="kp-sugg-item" href="'+p.url+'">';
        h+='<img class="kp-sugg-thumb" src="'+(p.thumb||'')+'" alt="" loading="lazy" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">';
        h+='<div class="kp-sugg-info"><div class="kp-sugg-title">'+titleHL+'</div>';
        if(p.label) h+='<div class="kp-sugg-label"><svg width="9" height="9" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M20.59 13.41l-7.17 7.17a2 2 0 0 1-2.83 0L2 12V2h10l8.59 8.59a2 2 0 0 1 0 2.82z"/><line x1="7" y1="7" x2="7.01" y2="7"/></svg>'+p.label+'</div>';
        h+='</div></a>';
      });
      kpSuggestBox.innerHTML=h;
      kpSuggestBox.classList.add('open');
    }

    function _kpShowHistory(){
      if(!kpSuggestBox) return;
      var hist=_kpGetHistory();
      if(!hist.length) return;
      var h='<div class="kp-sugg-history-head"><i class="fa-solid fa-clock-rotate-left"></i> گەڕانی پێشووت<button class="kp-sugg-history-clear" onclick="(function(){'+
        'try{localStorage.removeItem(\''+_KP_HIST_KEY+'\');}catch(e){}'+
        'document.getElementById(\'kp-suggestions\').classList.remove(\'open\');'+
        '})()">سڕینەوە</button></div>';
      hist.forEach(function(q){
        h+='<a class="kp-sugg-item" href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="document.getElementById(\'search-input\').value=\''+q.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+"';document.getElementById('search-input').dispatchEvent(new Event('input'))\">";
        h+='<div class="kp-sugg-info"><div class="kp-sugg-title"><i class="fa-solid fa-magnifying-glass" style="font-size:11px;margin-left:6px;color:var(--text-muted)"></i>'+q+'</div></div></a>';
      });
      kpSuggestBox.innerHTML=h;
      kpSuggestBox.classList.add('open');
    }

    function _kpFetchSug(q){
      if(_suggestCache[q]!==undefined){_kpShowSug(_suggestCache[q],q);return;}
      if(kpSuggestBox){kpSuggestBox.innerHTML='<div class="kp-sugg-spinner"></div>';kpSuggestBox.classList.add('open');}
      fetch(window.location.origin+'/feeds/posts/default?q='+encodeURIComponent(q)+'&max-results=8&alt=json')
        .then(function(r){return r.json();})
        .then(function(d){
          var entries=(d.feed&&d.feed.entry)||[];
          var res=entries.map(function(e){
            var url='';(e.link||[]).forEach(function(l){if(l.rel==='alternate')url=l.href;});
            var thumb='';
            if(e['media$thumbnail']) thumb=e['media$thumbnail'].url.replace(/\/s[0-9]+-c\//,'/s120-c/');
            else{var m=(e.content&&e.content.$t||'').match(/youtube\.com\/vi\/([^\/]+)\//);if(m)thumb='https://i.ytimg.com/vi/'+m[1]+'/mqdefault.jpg';}
            return{title:(e.title&&e.title.$t)||'',url:url,thumb:thumb,
              label:(e.category&&e.category[0]&&e.category[0].term)||''};
          });
          _suggestCache[q]=res;_kpShowSug(res,q);
        })
        .catch(function(){if(kpSuggestBox){kpSuggestBox.innerHTML='<div class="kp-sugg-empty">گەڕان سەرکەوتوو نەبوو، دووبارە هەوڵ بدەرەوە</div>';kpSuggestBox.classList.add('open');}});
    }

    // ── Keyboard Navigation ──
    function _kpKbdMove(dir){
      if(!kpSuggestBox||!kpSuggestBox.classList.contains('open')) return;
      var items=kpSuggestBox.querySelectorAll('.kp-sugg-item');
      if(!items.length) return;
      items[_kbdIdx]&&items[_kbdIdx].classList.remove('kp-kbd-active');
      _kbdIdx=(_kbdIdx+dir+items.length)%items.length;
      items[_kbdIdx].classList.add('kp-kbd-active');
      items[_kbdIdx].scrollIntoView({block:'nearest'});
    }

    if(si){
      si.addEventListener('input',function(){
        clearTimeout(_suggestTimer);
        _kbdIdx=-1;
        var q=this.value.trim();
        if(q.length<3){if(kpSuggestBox)kpSuggestBox.classList.remove('open');return;}
        _suggestTimer=setTimeout(function(){_kpFetchSug(q);},280);
      });
      si.addEventListener('focus',function(){
        if(!this.value.trim()) _kpShowHistory();
      });
      si.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){
        if(e.key==='ArrowDown'){e.preventDefault();_kpKbdMove(1);}
        else if(e.key==='ArrowUp'){e.preventDefault();_kpKbdMove(-1);}
        else if(e.key==='Enter'){
          if(kpSuggestBox){
            var active=kpSuggestBox.querySelector('.kp-kbd-active');
            if(active&&active.href&&active.href!==location.href){
              var q=si.value.trim();
              if(q) _kpSaveHistory(q);
              location.href=active.href;e.preventDefault();
            }
          }
        }
      });
      si.addEventListener('blur',function(){setTimeout(function(){if(kpSuggestBox)kpSuggestBox.classList.remove('open');},220);});
    }
    document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
      if(kpSuggestBox&&!kpSuggestBox.contains(e.target)&&e.target!==si)
        kpSuggestBox.classList.remove('open');
    });
    var dr=document.getElementById('drawer');
    var dov=document.getElementById('drawer-overlay');
    var od=document.getElementById('open-drawer');
    var cd=document.getElementById('close-drawer');
    function openD(){if(!dr)return;dr.classList.add('active');if(dov)dov.classList.add('active');if(od)od.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');document.body.style.overflow='hidden';}
    function closeD(){if(!dr)return;dr.classList.remove('active');if(dov)dov.classList.remove('active');if(od)od.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');document.body.style.overflow='';}
    if(od)od.addEventListener('click',openD);
    if(cd)cd.addEventListener('click',closeD);
    if(dov)dov.addEventListener('click',closeD);
    document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){if(e.key==='Escape'&&dr&&dr.classList.contains('active'))closeD();});
    var btt=document.getElementById('back-to-top');
    var bttFill=document.querySelector('.btt-fill');
    var CIRC=175.9;
    if(btt){window.addEventListener('scroll',function(){var show=window.scrollY>120;btt.classList.toggle('show',show);if(bttFill){var dh=document.documentElement.scrollHeight-window.innerHeight;var pct=dh>0?(window.scrollY/dh):0;bttFill.style.strokeDashoffset=CIRC*(1-pct);}},{passive:true});btt.addEventListener('click',function(){window.scrollTo({top:0,behavior:'smooth'});});}
    var pg=document.getElementById('scroll-progress');
    if(pg)window.addEventListener('scroll',function(){var dh=document.documentElement.scrollHeight-window.innerHeight;pg.style.width=(dh>0?(window.scrollY/dh)*100:0)+'%';},{passive:true});
  })();
  function copyPostUrl(btn){
    var orig=btn.innerHTML;
    function done(){btn.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid fa-check"></i> کۆپی کرا!';btn.style.cssText='background:#16a34a;color:#fff;border-color:#16a34a';setTimeout(function(){btn.innerHTML=orig;btn.style.cssText='';},2000);}
    if(navigator.clipboard){navigator.clipboard.writeText(window.location.href).then(done).catch(function(){var t=document.createElement('textarea');t.value=window.location.href;document.body.appendChild(t);t.select();document.execCommand('copy');document.body.removeChild(t);done();});}
    else{var t=document.createElement('textarea');t.value=window.location.href;document.body.appendChild(t);t.select();document.execCommand('copy');document.body.removeChild(t);done();}
  }

  /* ── ئینستاگرام: Web Share API (شیت نیشان دات) — ئەگەر نەگریا، کۆپیکردن ── */
  window.kpShareInstagram = function(btn){
    var title = document.title || 'کوڕی پاک';
    var url   = window.location.href;
    if(navigator.share){
      navigator.share({title: title, url: url})
        .catch(function(){});
    } else {
      /* fallback — کۆپیکردنی بەستەر */
      if(navigator.clipboard){
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(url).then(function(){
          kpToast && kpToast('<i class="fa-brands fa-instagram" style="margin-left:4px"></i> بەستەرەکە کۆپی کرا — پەستیش بکە لە ئینستاگرام');
        });
      }
    }
  };


    // ══ SVG بەجێی ئیمۆجی لەناو ناوەڕۆکی پۆستەکان ══
    var INFO_SVG='<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="20" height="20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" style="display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;color:var(--primary);margin-left:5px;margin-bottom:2px"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><line x1="12" y1="16" x2="12" y2="12"/><line x1="12" y1="8" x2="12.01" y2="8"/></svg>';
    var CLIP_SVG='<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="20" height="20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" style="display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;color:var(--accent);margin-left:5px;margin-bottom:2px"><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"/><rect x="8" y="2" width="8" height="4" rx="1" ry="1"/><line x1="9" y1="12" x2="15" y2="12"/><line x1="9" y1="16" x2="13" y2="16"/></svg>';
    function replacePostEmojis(root){
      if(!root) return;
      root.querySelectorAll('h2,h3,h4').forEach(function(el){
        el.innerHTML=el.innerHTML
          .replace(/\u2139\uFE0F|\u2139/g,INFO_SVG)
          .replace(/\uD83D\uDCCB/g,CLIP_SVG);
      });
    }
    (function(){
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){
        var pb=document.getElementById('post-body-container');
        if(pb) replacePostEmojis(pb);
      });
      var _eObs=new MutationObserver(function(muts){
        muts.forEach(function(m){
          m.addedNodes.forEach(function(n){if(n.nodeType===1) replacePostEmojis(n);});
        });
      });
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){
        var pb=document.getElementById('post-body-container');
        if(pb) _eObs.observe(pb,{childList:true,subtree:true});
      });
    })();


  /* ══ Ripple Effect — Vue/React style ══ */
  (function(){
    var RIPPLE_SELECTORS = '.kp-fb-btn,.srv-btn,.paging-button,.kp-auth-btn,.kp-google-btn,.kp-lib-tab,.kp-dd-item,.share-btn';
    document.addEventListener('pointerdown', function(e){
      var btn = e.target.closest(RIPPLE_SELECTORS);
      if(!btn) return;
      var r = btn.getBoundingClientRect();
      var el = document.createElement('span');
      el.className = 'kp-ripple-el';
      el.style.left = (e.clientX - r.left) + 'px';
      el.style.top  = (e.clientY - r.top)  + 'px';
      btn.appendChild(el);
      el.addEventListener('animationend', function(){ el.remove(); });
    });
  })();

  /* ══ Intersection Observer — کارتەکان تەنها کاتێ ئەنیمەیشن دەکەن کە دیاری دەبن ══ */
  (function(){
    if(!('IntersectionObserver' in window)) return;
    var obs = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
      entries.forEach(function(en){
        if(en.isIntersecting){
          en.target.style.animationPlayState = 'running';
          obs.unobserve(en.target);
        }
      });
    }, {threshold: 0.08});
    document.querySelectorAll('.post-card-item').forEach(function(el){
      el.style.animationPlayState = 'paused';
      obs.observe(el);
    });
  })();
  //]]>
  </script>
<!-- &#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552; سکریپتی وەرگێڕانی ناوی لەیبڵ &#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472;&#9472; چۆن بەکاری بهێنیت: لەنێو labelMap خوارەوە بنووسە: 'ناوی ئینگلیزی (هەمان ناوی لە Blogger)': 'ناوی کوردی', نموونە: 'Tafseer-1-2026': 'تەفسییر بەشی یەکەم' لینکەکان بەئینگلیزی دەمێننەوە&#1548; تەنها نووسینی سەر ڕووکار دەگۆڕێت. &#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552;&#9552; -->
<script type="text/javascript">
  //<![CDATA[
  (function(){
    // ══ خشتەی وەرگێڕان — ئەمانە بگۆڕە بەپێی پۆلینەکانی خۆت ══
        // خشتەی لەیبڵ بۆ هەموو زمانەکان
    var labelMaps = {
      'ckb': { 'Aqidda':'عەقیدە', 'Tafseer-1-2026':'تەفسییر بەشی یەکەم','Wtary Hainy':'وتاری هەینی ٢٠٢٦', 'Riyadh Al-Salehin':'باخچەی چاکە کاران','Sermons':'وتارەکان','Playlist':'زنجیرە وتارەکان' }
      // ── پۆلینی تر لێرەوە زیاد بکە ──
    };

    function translateLabels(lang){
      var map = labelMaps[lang] || labelMaps['ckb'];
      document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="/search/label/"]').forEach(function(a){
        var m = a.href.match(/\/search\/label\/([^?&#]+)/);
        if(!m) return;
        var raw = decodeURIComponent(m[1]);
        if(!a.dataset.origLabel) a.dataset.origLabel = raw;
        var orig = a.dataset.origLabel;
        var translated = map[orig] || map[a.textContent.trim()] || orig;
        if(a.children.length === 0){ a.textContent = translated; }
        else { a.childNodes.forEach(function(n){ if(n.nodeType===3 && n.textContent.trim()) n.textContent = translated; }); }
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.page-header h1, .bc-current').forEach(function(el){
        if(!el.dataset.origLabel) el.dataset.origLabel = el.textContent.trim();
        var t = map[el.dataset.origLabel];
        if(t) el.textContent = t;
      });
    }

    if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){ translateLabels('ckb'); });
    } else {
      translateLabels('ckb');
    }
  })();
  //]]>
  </script>

        'نوێترین وانەکان و وتارەکان ببینە لەسەر تێلیگرام':'نوێترین وانە و وتارەکان لە تەلەگرام ببینە',
        'شوێن بکەوە':'بەشداریکردن',
