var _replyTo=null; // {id, name}

function kpSetReply(commentId, authorName){
  _replyTo={id:commentId, name:authorName};
  var ind=document.getElementById('kp-reply-indicator');
  var nm=document.getElementById('kp-reply-name');
  if(ind){ ind.style.display='flex'; }
  if(nm) nm.textContent='وەڵامدانەوەی '+authorName;
  var input=document.getElementById('kp-cmt-input');
  if(input) input.focus();
  if(!kpUser) kpShowAuth();
  var form=document.getElementById('kp-cmt-form');
  if(form) form.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'center'});
}
window.kpSetReply=kpSetReply;

function kpCancelReply(){
  _replyTo=null;
  var ind=document.getElementById('kp-reply-indicator');
  if(ind) ind.style.display='none';
}
window.kpCancelReply=kpCancelReply;

function kpToggleSpoiler(wrap){
  wrap.classList.toggle('revealed');
}
window.kpToggleSpoiler=kpToggleSpoiler;

/* ── نوێکردنەوەی renderComments بۆ Replies + Spoiler ── */
function renderComments(docs, list, pid) {
  if(!docs||!docs.length){
    list.innerHTML='<div class="kp-cmt-empty"><i class="fa-regular fa-comments"></i><span>هێشتا هیچ لێدوانێک نییە. ببە بە یەکەم کەس!</span></div>';
    return;
  }
  /* جیاکردنەوەی کۆمێنتەکانی سەرەکی و وەڵامەکان */
  var topLevel=[];
  var replies={};
  docs.forEach(function(doc){
    var parentId=getF(doc,'parentId')||'';
    if(parentId){
      if(!replies[parentId]) replies[parentId]=[];
      replies[parentId].push(doc);
    } else {
      topLevel.push(doc);
    }
  });

  list.innerHTML = topLevel.map(function(doc){
    var id    = docId(doc);
    var rawText = getF(doc,'text')||'';
    var isSpoiler = getF(doc,'spoiler')||false;
    var text  = escH(rawText);
    var name  = escH(getF(doc,'displayName')||'بەکارهێنەر');
    var photo = escH(getF(doc,'photo')||getF(doc,'photoURL')||'');
    var ts    = getF(doc,'createdAt')||'';
    var likes = getF(doc,'likesCount')||0;
    var uid   = getF(doc,'userId')||'';
    var isOwn = kpUser && kpUser.uid===uid;
    var av = photo ? '<img src="'+photo+'" alt="" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">' : '<span>'+name.charAt(0)+'</span>';
    var textHtml = isSpoiler
      ? '<div class="kp-spoiler-wrap" onclick="kpToggleSpoiler(this)"><p class="kp-cmt-text kp-spoiler-text">'+text+'</p><div class="kp-spoiler-overlay"><i class="fa-solid fa-eye-slash"></i> سپۆیلەر — کرتە بکە بۆ بینین</div></div>'
      : '<p class="kp-cmt-text">'+text+'</p>';

    /* وەڵامەکانی ئەم کۆمێنتە */
    var repArr=replies[id]||[];
    var repHtml='';
    if(repArr.length){
      var rItems=repArr.map(function(rd){
        var rid=docId(rd);
        var rtext=escH(getF(rd,'text')||'');
        var rname=escH(getF(rd,'displayName')||'بەکارهێنەر');
        var rphoto=escH(getF(rd,'photo')||'');
        var rts=getF(rd,'createdAt')||'';
        var ruid=getF(rd,'userId')||'';
        var risOwn=kpUser&&kpUser.uid===ruid;
        var rav=rphoto?'<img src="'+rphoto+'" alt="" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">':'<span>'+rname.charAt(0)+'</span>';
        var risSpoiler=getF(rd,'spoiler')||false;
        var rtextHtml=risSpoiler
          ?'<div class="kp-spoiler-wrap" onclick="kpToggleSpoiler(this)"><p class="kp-cmt-text kp-spoiler-text">'+rtext+'</p><div class="kp-spoiler-overlay"><i class="fa-solid fa-eye-slash"></i> سپۆیلەر — کرتە بکە بۆ بینین</div></div>'
          :'<p class="kp-cmt-text">'+rtext+'</p>';
        return '<div class="kp-cmt-reply-item" data-id="'+rid+'">'+
          '<div class="kp-cmt-avatar" style="width:30px;height:30px;font-size:12px">'+rav+'</div>'+
          '<div class="kp-cmt-body">'+
            '<div class="kp-cmt-header">'+
              '<strong>'+rname+'</strong>'+
              '<span class="kp-cmt-time">'+relTime(rts)+'</span>'+
              (risOwn?'<button class="kp-cmt-del" onclick="kpDelComment(\''+rid+'\')" title="سڕینەوە"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button>':'')+
            '</div>'+rtextHtml+
          '</div>'+
        '</div>';
      }).join('');
      repHtml='<div class="kp-cmt-replies">'+rItems+'</div>';
    }

    return '<div class="kp-cmt-item" data-id="'+id+'">' +
      '<div class="kp-cmt-avatar">'+av+'</div>' +
      '<div class="kp-cmt-body">' +
        '<div class="kp-cmt-header">' +
          '<strong>'+name+'</strong>' +
          '<span class="kp-cmt-time">'+relTime(ts)+'</span>' +
          (isOwn?'<button class="kp-cmt-del" onclick="kpDelComment(\''+id+'\')" title="سڕینەوە"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button>':'') +
        '</div>' +
        textHtml +
        '<div class="kp-cmt-actions">' +
          '<button class="kp-cmt-like-btn" data-id="'+id+'" data-likes="'+likes+'" onclick="kpLikeComment(this,\''+pid+'\')">' +
            '<i class="fa-regular fa-heart"></i> <span>'+likes+'</span>' +
          '</button>' +
          '<button class="kp-cmt-reply-btn" onclick="kpSetReply(\''+id+'\',\''+name+'\')">' +
            '<i class="fa-solid fa-reply"></i> وەڵام' +
          '</button>' +
          (repArr.length?'<button class="kp-replies-toggle" onclick="this.closest(\'.kp-cmt-item\').querySelector(\'.kp-cmt-replies\').style.display=this.closest(\'.kp-cmt-item\').querySelector(\'.kp-cmt-replies\').style.display===\'none\'?\'flex\':\'none\'"><i class="fa-solid fa-comments"></i> '+repArr.length+' وەڵام</button>':'') +
        '</div>' +
        repHtml +
      '</div>' +
    '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

/* ── نوێکردنەوەی kpSubmitComment بۆ پشتگیری parentId + spoiler ── */
function kpSubmitComment() {
  if(!kpUser){ kpShowAuth(); return; }
  var input=document.getElementById('kp-cmt-input');
  var text=(input&&input.value||'').trim();
  if(!text) return;
  var pid=getPostId(); if(!pid) return;
  var isSpoiler=document.getElementById('kp-spoiler-chk')&&document.getElementById('kp-spoiler-chk').checked;
  var btn=document.getElementById('kp-cmt-submit');
  if(btn){ btn.disabled=true; btn.textContent='ناردن...'; }
  var data={
    text:strV(text),
    userId:strV(kpUser.uid),
    displayName:strV(kpUser.name),
    photo:strV(kpUser.photo||''),
    createdAt:tsV(),
    likesCount:numV(0),
    spoiler:boolV(!!isSpoiler)
  };
  if(_replyTo&&_replyTo.id) data.parentId=strV(_replyTo.id);
  var savedText=text;
  var savedSpoiler=!!isSpoiler;
  var savedReplyId=_replyTo&&_replyTo.id?_replyTo.id:null;

  getToken().then(function(tok){
    if(!tok){ kpShowAuth(); return; }
    return fsAdd('posts/'+pid+'/comments',data,tok).then(function(){
      /* ١. دەستبەجێ input پاک بکەرەوە */
      if(input) input.value='';
      var spChk=document.getElementById('kp-spoiler-chk');
      if(spChk) spChk.checked=false;
      kpCancelReply();
      /* ٢. Optimistic UI — پێش هەر reload ── دەستبەجێ نیشان بدە */
      _kpOptimisticAdd(savedText, savedSpoiler, savedReplyId);
      kpToast('لێدوانەکەت زیادکرا ✓');
      /* ٣. لە پشتەوە (silent) reload — ئەگەر سەرکەوت optimistic جێگرێتەوە */
      _cmtLoaded=false;
      setTimeout(function(){ loadComments(true); }, 1000);
    });
  }).finally(function(){
    if(btn){ btn.disabled=false; btn.innerHTML='<i class="fa-solid fa-paper-plane"></i> ناردن'; }
  });
}
window.kpSubmitComment = kpSubmitComment;

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════
   BOOT — AES-256-GCM Key Decryption → Firebase Init
   تەشفیرگشاوەی کلیلەکان پێش دەستپێکردنی Firebase
══════════════════════════════════════════════ */
(function initApp(){
  var FB_VER = '10.11.0';
  var BASE = 'https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/'+FB_VER+'/';

  /* گامی یەکەم: کلیلەکان تەشفیرگشا بکە */
  Promise.all([
    _kpDecrypt(_KP_ENC.f),
    _kpDecrypt(_KP_ENC.i)
  ]).then(function(keys){
    FB_API_KEY  = keys[0];
    IMGBB_KEY   = keys[1];
  }).catch(function(){
    /* ئەگەر WebCrypto بەردەست نەبوو — fallback نییە (بەمەرامی بۆ ئەمنیەت) */
    console.warn('KP: WebCrypto بەردەست نییە');
  }).then(function(){
    /* گامی دووەم: Firebase SDK بار بکە */
    return Promise.all([
      _loadScript(BASE+'firebase-app-compat.js'),
      _loadScript(BASE+'firebase-auth-compat.js')
    ]);
  }).then(function(){

    if(!FB_API_KEY){ console.warn('KP: کلیلی Firebase نەگەیشت'); return; }

    /* ── Init App (یەک جار) ── */
    if(!firebase.apps.length){
      firebase.initializeApp({
        apiKey:      FB_API_KEY,
        authDomain:  FB_AUTH_DOMAIN,
        projectId:   FB_PROJECT
      });
    }

    /* ── LOCAL Persistence ── */
    firebase.auth().setPersistence(
      firebase.auth.Auth.Persistence.LOCAL
    ).catch(function(){});

    /* ── Auth Listener ── */
    setupAuthListener();

    /* ── پۆستی تاک: لایک + کۆمێنت + هەڵسەنگاندن ── */
    var pid=getPostId();
    if(pid){
      loadPostLikes();
      kpInitRating();
      var cmtSection=document.getElementById('kp-firebase-comments');
      if(cmtSection){
        if('IntersectionObserver' in window){
          var obs=new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
            if(entries[0].isIntersecting){ loadComments(); obs.disconnect(); }
          },{threshold:0.05});
          obs.observe(cmtSection);
        } else {
          loadComments();
        }
      }
    }

  }).catch(function(err){
    console.warn('KP: Firebase SDK بارنەکرا', err);
  });
})();

})();
//]]>
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
(function(){
'use strict';

/* ── SW جێگیرکردن ── */
var SW_URL = 'https://kuripak2026.blogspot.com/p/sw.html';

if('serviceWorker' in navigator){
  window.addEventListener('load', function(){
    navigator.serviceWorker.register(SW_URL, {scope:'/'})
      .then(function(reg){
        console.log('KP SW: تۆمارکرا', reg.scope);
        reg.addEventListener('updatefound', function(){
          var nw = reg.installing;
          if(!nw) return;
          nw.addEventListener('statechange', function(){
            if(nw.state==='installed' && navigator.serviceWorker.controller){
              kpToast && kpToast('<img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns%3D%22http%3A%2F%2Fwww.w3.org%2F2000%2Fsvg%22%20viewBox%3D%220%200%2032%2032%22%3E%0A%20%20%3Cdefs%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3ClinearGradient%20id%3D%22rg%22%20x1%3D%220%22%20y1%3D%220%22%20x2%3D%221%22%20y2%3D%221%22%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%20%20%3Cstop%20offset%3D%220%25%22%20stop-color%3D%22%2360d8ff%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%20%20%3Cstop%20offset%3D%2250%25%22%20stop-color%3D%22%231b9ed4%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%20%20%3Cstop%20offset%3D%22100%25%22%20stop-color%3D%22%230d6ba0%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3C%2FlinearGradient%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3Cfilter%20id%3D%22rf%22%3E%3CfeDropShadow%20dx%3D%220%22%20dy%3D%221%22%20stdDeviation%3D%221.5%22%20flood-color%3D%22%230d6ba0%22%20flood-opacity%3D%22.5%22%2F%3E%3C%2Ffilter%3E%0A%20%20%3C%2Fdefs%3E%0A%20%20%3Cg%20filter%3D%22url%28%23rf%29%22%20fill%3D%22none%22%20stroke%3D%22url%28%23rg%29%22%20stroke-width%3D%223.2%22%20stroke-linecap%3D%22round%22%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3Cpath%20d%3D%22M8%2016%20A8%208%200%201%201%2016%2024%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3Cpolyline%20points%3D%2210%2C28%2016%2C24%2010%2C20%22%20fill%3D%22url%28%23rg%29%22%20stroke%3D%22none%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3Cpath%20d%3D%22M24%2016%20A8%208%200%201%201%2016%208%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3Cpolyline%20points%3D%2222%2C4%2016%2C8%2022%2C12%22%20fill%3D%22url%28%23rg%29%22%20stroke%3D%22none%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%3C%2Fg%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E" style="width:1.1em;height:1.1em;vertical-align:-.18em;display:inline-block" alt="refresh"/> نوێکردنەوەی ماڵپەڕ بەردەستە — پەڕەکە نوێبکەرەوە');
            }
          });
        });
      })
      .catch(function(err){ console.warn('KP SW: تۆمارنەکرا', err); });
  });

/* ── Offline/Online Detection ── */
(function(){
  var _offBanner=document.getElementById('kp-offline-banner');
  function _checkOnline(){
    if(!_offBanner) return;
    if(!navigator.onLine){ _offBanner.classList.add('show'); }
    else { _offBanner.classList.remove('show'); }
  }
  window.addEventListener('online',  _checkOnline);
  window.addEventListener('offline', _checkOnline);
  _checkOnline();
})();

/* ── PWA Install Banner ── */
var _deferredPrompt = null;
var banner     = document.getElementById('kp-pwa-banner');
var installBtn = document.getElementById('kp-pwa-install-btn');
var dismissBtn = document.getElementById('kp-pwa-dismiss-btn');
var PWA_KEY    = 'kp_pwa_dismissed';
var PWA_VER    = 'v5'; /* ئەمە بگۆڕە کاتێک نوێی دەکەیتەوە */
/* ئەگەر ڤێرژنی نوێ بوو، کلیدی داخستنەوەی کۆنەکە پاک بکەرەوە */
if(localStorage.getItem('kp_pwa_ver') !== PWA_VER){
  localStorage.removeItem(PWA_KEY);
  localStorage.setItem('kp_pwa_ver', PWA_VER);

  }

function _isPWAInstalled(){
  if(window.matchMedia('(display-mode: standalone)').matches) return true;
  if(window.navigator.standalone === true) return true;
  return false;
}

function showBanner(){
  if(!banner) return;
  if(localStorage.getItem(PWA_KEY)) return;
  if(_isPWAInstalled()) return;
  setTimeout(function(){ banner.classList.add('visible'); }, 2500);
}

/* Chrome/Edge: prompt ئینلاین */
window.addEventListener('beforeinstallprompt', function(e){
  e.preventDefault();
  _deferredPrompt = e;
  showBanner(); /* ئێستا پڕۆمپتەکە ئامادەیە */
});

/* Fallback: ئەگەر beforeinstallprompt فایەر نەکرد (iOS / Chrome دواخستووە)
   بانەر دەربهێنە — دوگمەکە ڕێنمایی دەستی دەدات */
window.addEventListener('load', function(){
  if(!_isPWAInstalled() && !localStorage.getItem(PWA_KEY)){
    setTimeout(function(){
      if(!_deferredPrompt) showBanner(); /* fallback بێ prompt */
    }, 4000);
  }
});

if(installBtn){
  installBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    if(_deferredPrompt){
      /* ── کرۆم/ئێدج: prompt ئینلاین ── */
      banner.classList.remove('visible');
      _deferredPrompt.prompt();
      _deferredPrompt.userChoice.then(function(res){
        if(res.outcome === 'accepted'){
          kpToast && kpToast('<img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns%3D%22http%3A%2F%2Fwww.w3.org%2F2000%2Fsvg%22%20viewBox%3D%220%200%2032%2032%22%3E%0A%20%20%3Cdefs%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3CradialGradient%20id%3D%22cg%22%20cx%3D%2240%25%22%20cy%3D%2235%25%22%20r%3D%2265%25%22%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%20%20%3Cstop%20offset%3D%220%25%22%20stop-color%3D%22%234ee8b4%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%20%20%3Cstop%20offset%3D%22100%25%22%20stop-color%3D%22%230fa86a%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3C%2FradialGradient%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3Cfilter%20id%3D%22glow%22%3E%3CfeGaussianBlur%20stdDeviation%3D%221.2%22%20result%3D%22b%22%2F%3E%3CfeMerge%3E%3CfeMergeNode%20in%3D%22b%22%2F%3E%3CfeMergeNode%20in%3D%22SourceGraphic%22%2F%3E%3C%2FfeMerge%3E%3C%2Ffilter%3E%0A%20%20%3C%2Fdefs%3E%0A%20%20%3Ccircle%20cx%3D%2216%22%20cy%3D%2216%22%20r%3D%2215%22%20fill%3D%22url%28%23cg%29%22%20filter%3D%22url%28%23glow%29%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%3Ccircle%20cx%3D%2216%22%20cy%3D%2216%22%20r%3D%2215%22%20fill%3D%22none%22%20stroke%3D%22rgba%28255%2C255%2C255%2C.35%29%22%20stroke-width%3D%221.2%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%3Ccircle%20cx%3D%2216%22%20cy%3D%2216%22%20r%3D%2212%22%20fill%3D%22none%22%20stroke%3D%22rgba%28255%2C255%2C255%2C.15%29%22%20stroke-width%3D%22.8%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%3Cpolyline%20points%3D%228%2C16%2013%2C22%2024%2C10%22%20fill%3D%22none%22%20stroke%3D%22%23fff%22%20stroke-width%3D%222.8%22%20stroke-linecap%3D%22round%22%20stroke-linejoin%3D%22round%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%3Cellipse%20cx%3D%2212%22%20cy%3D%2212%22%20rx%3D%223%22%20ry%3D%221.5%22%20fill%3D%22rgba%28255%2C255%2C255%2C.18%29%22%20transform%3D%22rotate%28-30%2C12%2C12%29%22%2F%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E" style="width:1.1em;height:1.1em;vertical-align:-.18em;display:inline-block" alt="check"/> ئەپەکە دامەزرا! بەخێربێیت');
          localStorage.setItem(PWA_KEY, '1');
        }
        _deferredPrompt = null;
      });
    } else {
      /* ── Fallback: ڕێنمایی دەستی ── */
      var isIOS = /iphone|ipad|ipod/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
      if(isIOS){
        kpToast && kpToast('لە Safari: Share ← زیادکردن بۆ شاشەی سەرەکی');
      } else {
        kpToast && kpToast('⋮ لیست ← "زیادکردن بۆ شاشەی سەرەکی" کرتە بکە');
      }
      banner.classList.remove('visible');
      localStorage.setItem(PWA_KEY, '1');
    }
  });
}

if(dismissBtn){
  dismissBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    banner.classList.remove('visible');
    localStorage.setItem(PWA_KEY, '1');
  });
}

  banner.classList.remove('visible');
  kpToast && kpToast('<img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns%3D%22http%3A%2F%2Fwww.w3.org%2F2000%2Fsvg%22%20viewBox%3D%220%200%2032%2032%22%3E%0A%20%20%3Cdefs%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3CradialGradient%20id%3D%22cg%22%20cx%3D%2240%25%22%20cy%3D%2235%25%22%20r%3D%2265%25%22%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%20%20%3Cstop%20offset%3D%220%25%22%20stop-color%3D%22%234ee8b4%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%20%20%3Cstop%20offset%3D%22100%25%22%20stop-color%3D%22%230fa86a%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3C%2FradialGradient%3E%0A%20%20%20%20%3Cfilter%20id%3D%22glow%22%3E%3CfeGaussianBlur%20stdDeviation%3D%221.2%22%20result%3D%22b%22%2F%3E%3CfeMerge%3E%3CfeMergeNode%20in%3D%22b%22%2F%3E%3CfeMergeNode%20in%3D%22SourceGraphic%22%2F%3E%3C%2FfeMerge%3E%3C%2Ffilter%3E%0A%20%20%3C%2Fdefs%3E%0A%20%20%3Ccircle%20cx%3D%2216%22%20cy%3D%2216%22%20r%3D%2215%22%20fill%3D%22url%28%23cg%29%22%20filter%3D%22url%28%23glow%29%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%3Ccircle%20cx%3D%2216%22%20cy%3D%2216%22%20r%3D%2215%22%20fill%3D%22none%22%20stroke%3D%22rgba%28255%2C255%2C255%2C.35%29%22%20stroke-width%3D%221.2%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%3Ccircle%20cx%3D%2216%22%20cy%3D%2216%22%20r%3D%2212%22%20fill%3D%22none%22%20stroke%3D%22rgba%28255%2C255%2C255%2C.15%29%22%20stroke-width%3D%22.8%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%3Cpolyline%20points%3D%228%2C16%2013%2C22%2024%2C10%22%20fill%3D%22none%22%20stroke%3D%22%23fff%22%20stroke-width%3D%222.8%22%20stroke-linecap%3D%22round%22%20stroke-linejoin%3D%22round%22%2F%3E%0A%20%20%3Cellipse%20cx%3D%2212%22%20cy%3D%2212%22%20rx%3D%223%22%20ry%3D%221.5%22%20fill%3D%22rgba%28255%2C255%2C255%2C.18%29%22%20transform%3D%22rotate%28-30%2C12%2C12%29%22%2F%3E%0A%3C%2Fsvg%3E" style="width:1.1em;height:1.1em;vertical-align:-.18em;display:inline-block" alt="check"/> ئەپەکە دامەزرا!');
  localStorage.setItem(PWA_KEY, '1');

<!-- destroyAdButton JS سڕدراوەتەوە: CSS لەسەر ئاستی سەرەوە بەتەواوی کاردەکات -->
<!-- سەرەتای سکریپتی بەزۆر بەکارهێنانی پلەیەری ناوخۆیی -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    var postBody = document.getElementById('post-body-container');
    if (!postBody) return;

    // گەڕان بەدوای هەموو ئایفرەیمەکاندا
    var iframes = postBody.querySelectorAll('iframe');
    // ئەو جۆرە ڤیدیۆیانەی کە پلەری خۆت دەتوانێت لێیان بدات
    var playableRegex = /\.(mp4|webm|m3u8|mkv|ogg|ogv|mov|avi)(\?[^"'\s]*)?$/i;

    iframes.forEach(function(iframe) {
        var src = iframe.src || '';

        // ١. ئەگەر یوتیوب بوو، وازی لێ بهێنە وەک خۆی بمێنێتەوە
        if (src.indexOf('youtube.com') > -1 || src.indexOf('youtu.be') > -1 || src.indexOf('youtube-nocookie.com') > -1) {
            return; 
        }

        // ٢. ئەگەر یوتیوب نەبوو، بزانە ئایا لینکی ڕاستەوخۆیە کراوە بە ئایفرەیم؟
        if (playableRegex.test(src)) {
            // داتا-ئەتریبیوت بەکارهێنراوە بەجێی hidden link — SEO-safe
            iframe.setAttribute('data-kp-src', src);
            iframe.remove(); // سڕینەوەی ئایفرەیمەکە بۆ ئەوەی پلەیەرەکەی خۆت جێگەی بگرێتەوە
        } else {
            // تێبینی: ئەگەر ئایفرەیمەکە Vidmoly بێت، لێرەدا دەمێنێتەوە چونکە MP4 نییە و کۆدی HTMLـە.
            // ئەگەر بتەوێت تەنانەت ڤیدمۆلیش تێکبشکێنێت (کە کارناکات)، دەتوانیت لە خوارەوە دەستکاری بکەیت.
        }
    });
});
//]]>
</script>

<!-- destroyJWControls JS سڕدراوەتەوە: CSS لەسەر ئاستی سەرەوە بەتەواوی کاردەکات -->
<!-- executeAdBlocker JS سڕدراوەتەوە: ئەم سکریپتە هەوڵی چوونە ناو iframe دەکرد (cross-origin XSS) کە گووگڵ وەک malware دەیبینی. CSS لەسەر ئاستی سەرەوە بەتەواوی کاردەکات. -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
// ── SORT POSTS ──
(function(){
  // مینیو بگوازە ناو body تا لە هەر stacking context دەرببێت
  function kpInitMenu(){
    var menu=document.getElementById('kpSortMenu');
    if(menu&&menu.parentNode!==document.body){
      document.body.appendChild(menu);
      menu.style.position='fixed';
      menu.style.display='none';
      menu.classList.remove('open');
    }
  }
  function kpPositionMenu(){
    var btn=document.getElementById('kpSortBtn');
    var menu=document.getElementById('kpSortMenu');
    if(!btn||!menu)return;
    var r=btn.getBoundingClientRect();
    var menuW=180;
    var left=r.left;
    if(left+menuW>window.innerWidth-8)left=r.right-menuW;
    if(left<8)left=8;
    menu.style.top=(r.bottom+6)+'px';
    menu.style.left=left+'px';
  }
  function kpOpenMenu(){
    var menu=document.getElementById('kpSortMenu');
    var btn=document.getElementById('kpSortBtn');
    if(!menu||!btn)return;
    kpPositionMenu();
    menu.style.display='block';
    btn.classList.add('kp-sort-open');
  }
  function kpCloseMenu(){
    var menu=document.getElementById('kpSortMenu');
    var btn=document.getElementById('kpSortBtn');
    if(menu)menu.style.display='none';
    if(btn)btn.classList.remove('kp-sort-open');
  }
  // ژمارەی عەرەبی (٠-٩) بگۆڕە بۆ ژمارەی ئینگلیزی
  function kpArabicToLatin(s){
    return (s||'').replace(/[٠-٩]/g,function(d){return d.charCodeAt(0)-1632;})
                  .replace(/[۰-۹]/g,function(d){return d.charCodeAt(0)-1776;});
  }
  // چوار وشەی یەکەم دەردەهێنێت بۆ ڕیزبەندی بەپێی ناو
  function kpFirstWords(str,n){
    return (str||'').trim().split(/\s+/).slice(0,n).join(' ');
  }
  // Natural sort — ژمارە وەک ژمارە
  function kpNatSort(a,b){
    var ra=kpArabicToLatin(kpFirstWords(a,4));
    var rb=kpArabicToLatin(kpFirstWords(b,4));
    var re=/(\d+)|(\D+)/g;
    var ta=ra.match(re)||[];
    var tb=rb.match(re)||[];
    for(var i=0;i<Math.max(ta.length,tb.length);i++){
      if(i>=ta.length)return -1;
      if(i>=tb.length)return 1;
      var na=parseInt(ta[i],10);
      var nb=parseInt(tb[i],10);
      if(!isNaN(na)&&!isNaN(nb)){
        if(na!==nb)return na-nb;
      }else{
        var c=ta[i].localeCompare(tb[i],'ku');
        if(c!==0)return c;
      }
    }
    return 0;
  }
  function kpDoSort(sortType){
    var grid=document.querySelector('.post-list-grid');
    if(!grid)return;
    var items=Array.prototype.slice.call(grid.querySelectorAll('.post-card-item'));
    items.sort(function(a,b){
      if(sortType==='date-desc')return new Date(b.dataset.date||0)-new Date(a.dataset.date||0);
      if(sortType==='date-asc')return new Date(a.dataset.date||0)-new Date(b.dataset.date||0);
      if(sortType==='title-asc')return kpNatSort(a.dataset.title,b.dataset.title);
      if(sortType==='title-desc')return kpNatSort(b.dataset.title,a.dataset.title);
      return 0;
    });
    items.forEach(function(el){grid.appendChild(el);});
    document.querySelectorAll('.kp-sort-opt').forEach(function(o){o.classList.remove('kp-sort-active');});
    var active=document.querySelector('.kp-sort-opt[data-sort="'+sortType+'"]');
    if(active)active.classList.add('kp-sort-active');
    kpCloseMenu();
  }
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    var btn=e.target.closest('#kpSortBtn');
    var opt=e.target.closest('.kp-sort-opt');
    var menu=document.getElementById('kpSortMenu');
    if(btn){
      e.stopPropagation();
      if(menu&&menu.style.display==='block')kpCloseMenu();
      else kpOpenMenu();
      return;
    }
    if(opt&&opt.dataset.sort){
      e.stopPropagation();
      kpDoSort(opt.dataset.sort);
      return;
    }
    if(menu&&menu.style.display==='block')kpCloseMenu();
  });
  // جێبەجێکردن کاتێ DOM ئامادەبوو
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',kpInitMenu);
  }else{
    kpInitMenu();
  }
})();
// ── KP GRID SWITCHER JS ──
(function(){
  'use strict';
  var STORE_KEY='kp_grid_cols';
  function kpGetGrid(){return document.getElementById('kpPostGrid')||document.querySelector('.post-list-grid');}
  function kpApplyCols(n){
    var grid=kpGetGrid();
    if(!grid)return;
    [1,2,3,4].forEach(function(c){grid.classList.remove('kp-cols-'+c);});
    grid.classList.add('kp-cols-'+n);
    document.querySelectorAll('.kp-grid-btn').forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('kp-grid-active',parseInt(b.dataset.cols,10)===n);
    });
    try{localStorage.setItem(STORE_KEY,n);}catch(e){}
  }
  function kpInitGrid(){
    var saved=1;
    try{var s=localStorage.getItem(STORE_KEY);if(s&&[1,2].indexOf(parseInt(s,10))>-1)saved=parseInt(s,10);}catch(e){}
    kpApplyCols(saved);
    document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
      var btn=e.target.closest('.kp-grid-btn');
      if(btn&&btn.dataset.cols){kpApplyCols(parseInt(btn.dataset.cols,10));}
    });
  }
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',kpInitGrid);}
  else{kpInitGrid();}
})();
//]]>
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
(function(){
'use strict';
/* ── Open / Close ── */
window.kpShowSettings=function(){
  document.getElementById('kp-settings-modal').classList.add('active');
  // بستنی مینیۆ
  var d=document.getElementById('drawer');
  var o=document.getElementById('drawer-overlay');
  if(d)d.classList.remove('active');
  if(o)o.classList.remove('active');
  kpSettingsInit();
};
window.kpCloseSettings=function(){
  document.getElementById('kp-settings-modal').classList.remove('active');
};

/* ── Init: بارکردنی ئەو ڕێکخستنانە کە پێشتر پاشەکەوت کراون ── */
function kpSettingsInit(){
  // ١ — قەبارەی فۆنت
  var fs=localStorage.getItem('kp_font_size')||'15';
  var r=document.getElementById('kp-font-range');
  var v=document.getElementById('kp-font-val');
  if(r){r.value=fs;} if(v){v.textContent=fs;}

  // ٢ — ستوونەکان
  var cols=parseInt(localStorage.getItem('kp_grid_cols')||'1',10);
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-set-section .kp-chip[data-cols]').forEach(function(c){
    c.classList.toggle('active',parseInt(c.dataset.cols,10)===cols);
  });

  // ٣ — فۆنت
  var cf=localStorage.getItem('kp_font')||'IBM Plex Sans Arabic';
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-font-chip').forEach(function(c){
    c.classList.toggle('active',c.dataset.font===cf);
  });

  // ٤ — سێرڤەرەکان
  var ytHide=localStorage.getItem('kp_srv_yt')==='0';
  var vmHide=localStorage.getItem('kp_srv_vm')==='0';
  var yt=document.getElementById('kp-srv-yt');
  var vm=document.getElementById('kp-srv-vm');
  if(yt)yt.checked=!ytHide;
  if(vm)vm.checked=!vmHide;

  // ٧ — ژێرنووس ڕەنگ
  var sc=localStorage.getItem('kp_sub_color')||'#ffffff';
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-sub-color').forEach(function(c){c.classList.toggle('active',c.dataset.color===sc);});
  // ژێرنووس قەبارە
  var ss=localStorage.getItem('kp_sub_size')||'17px';
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-sub-size').forEach(function(c){c.classList.toggle('active',c.dataset.size===ss);});
  // ژێرنووس پاڵاو
  var sb=localStorage.getItem('kp_sub_bg')||'rgba(0,0,0,0.7)';
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-sub-bg').forEach(function(c){c.classList.toggle('active',c.dataset.bg===sb);});
}

/* ── ١ قەبارەی فۆنت ── */
window.kpSetFontSize=function(val){
  document.getElementById('kp-font-val').textContent=val;
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('font-size',val+'px');
  document.body.style.fontSize=val+'px';
  localStorage.setItem('kp_font_size',val);
};

  if(fs){document.body.style.fontSize=fs+'px';}
})();

window.kpSettingCols=function(n){
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-set-section .kp-chip[data-cols]').forEach(function(c){
    c.classList.toggle('active',parseInt(c.dataset.cols,10)===n);
  });
  // نوێکردنەوەی هەردوو دوگمەی grid switcher
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-grid-btn[data-cols]').forEach(function(b){
    b.classList.toggle('kp-grid-active',parseInt(b.dataset.cols,10)===n);
  });
  var grid=document.getElementById('kpPostGrid')||document.querySelector('.post-list-grid');
  if(grid){[1,2,3,4].forEach(function(c){grid.classList.remove('kp-cols-'+c);});grid.classList.add('kp-cols-'+n);}

};

/* ── ٣ شێوازی فۆنت ── */
window.kpSetFont=function(el){
  var font=el.dataset.font;
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-font-chip').forEach(function(c){c.classList.remove('active');});
  el.classList.add('active');
  // بارکردنی فۆنت لە گووگڵ ئەگەر نەبوو
  var fontId='kp-gfont-'+font.replace(/\s/g,'_');
  if(!document.getElementById(fontId)){
    var lk=document.createElement('link');
    lk.id=fontId;lk.rel='stylesheet';
    lk.href='https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family='+encodeURIComponent(font)+':wght@400;600;700&display=swap';
    document.head.appendChild(lk);
  }
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--font-family',"'"+font+"', sans-serif");
  document.body.style.fontFamily="'"+font+"', sans-serif";
  localStorage.setItem('kp_font',font);
  kpToast('فۆنت گۆڕدرا ✓');
};
// جێبەجێکردن لە بارکردنی پەڕە
(function(){
  var cf=localStorage.getItem('kp_font');
  if(cf && cf!=='IBM Plex Sans Arabic'){
    var fontId='kp-gfont-'+cf.replace(/\s/g,'_');
    if(!document.getElementById(fontId)){
      var lk=document.createElement('link');
      lk.id=fontId;lk.rel='stylesheet';
      lk.href='https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family='+encodeURIComponent(cf)+':wght@400;600;700&display=swap';
      document.head.appendChild(lk);
    }
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--font-family',"'"+cf+"', sans-serif");
    document.body.style.fontFamily="'"+cf+"', sans-serif";
  }
})();

/* ── ٤ سێرڤەرەکان ── */
window.kpSrvToggle=function(){
  var ytOn=document.getElementById('kp-srv-yt').checked;
  var vmOn=document.getElementById('kp-srv-vm').checked;
  localStorage.setItem('kp_srv_yt',ytOn?'1':'0');
  localStorage.setItem('kp_srv_vm',vmOn?'1':'0');
  var b2=document.getElementById('srv-btn-2');
  var b1=document.getElementById('srv-btn-1');
  if(b2)b2.style.display=ytOn?'':'none';
  if(b1)b1.style.display=vmOn?'':'none';
  kpToast('ڕێکخستنەکان پاشەکەوت کران ✓');
};

(function(){
  var ytOn=localStorage.getItem('kp_srv_yt');
  var vmOn=localStorage.getItem('kp_srv_vm');
  if(ytOn==='0'){var b=document.getElementById('srv-btn-2');if(b)b.style.display='none';}
  if(vmOn==='0'){var b=document.getElementById('srv-btn-1');if(b)b.style.display='none';}
})();

/* ── ٦ گۆڕینی وشەی نهێنی ── */
window.kpSetChangePass=function(){
  var p1=document.getElementById('kp-set-np1').value;
  var p2=document.getElementById('kp-set-np2').value;
  var msg=document.getElementById('kp-set-pass-msg');
  msg.style.display='none';
  if(!p1||p1.length<6){msg.textContent='وشەی نهێنی دەبێت ٦ پیت یان زیاتر بێت';msg.style.display='block';return;}
  if(p1!==p2){msg.textContent='وشەی نهێنی و دووبارەکردنەوەکەی وەک یەک نین';msg.style.display='block';return;}
  // کارکردن لەگەل Firebase Auth ئەگەر بوو
  if(typeof firebase!=='undefined'&&firebase.auth&&firebase.auth().currentUser){
    firebase.auth().currentUser.updatePassword(p1).then(function(){
      kpToast('وشەی نهێنی گۆڕدرا ✓');
      document.getElementById('kp-set-np1').value='';
      document.getElementById('kp-set-np2').value='';
    }).catch(function(e){
      msg.textContent=e.message;msg.style.display='block';
    });
  } else {
    msg.textContent='تکایە پێشتر چوونەژوورەوە بکە';msg.style.display='block';
  }
};

/* ── ٧ ستایلی ژێرنووس ── */
var _kpSubCSS=null;
function kpApplySubStyle(){
  var color=localStorage.getItem('kp_sub_color')||'#ffffff';
  var size=localStorage.getItem('kp_sub_size')||'17px';
  var bg=localStorage.getItem('kp_sub_bg')||'rgba(0,0,0,0.7)';
  var css='::cue{color:'+color+';font-size:'+size+';background:'+bg+';padding:2px 6px;border-radius:4px}';
  if(!_kpSubCSS){_kpSubCSS=document.createElement('style');_kpSubCSS.id='kp-sub-css';document.head.appendChild(_kpSubCSS);}
  _kpSubCSS.textContent=css;
}
window.kpSubStyle=function(el,type){
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-sub-'+type).forEach(function(c){c.classList.remove('active');});
  el.classList.add('active');
  if(type==='color')localStorage.setItem('kp_sub_color',el.dataset.color);
  if(type==='size')localStorage.setItem('kp_sub_size',el.dataset.size);
  if(type==='bg')localStorage.setItem('kp_sub_bg',el.dataset.bg);
  kpApplySubStyle();
  kpToast('ستایلی ژێرنووس گۆڕدرا ✓');
};
kpApplySubStyle();

window.kpSetPrimary=function(el){
  var color=el.dataset.color;
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-color-dot').forEach(function(c){
    c.classList.toggle('active',c===el);
    c.style.outline=c===el?'2.5px solid var(--text-main)':'none';
    c.style.outlineOffset='2px';
  });
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--primary',color);
  var hex=color.replace('#','');
  var r=parseInt(hex.substring(0,2),16),g=parseInt(hex.substring(2,4),16),b=parseInt(hex.substring(4,6),16);
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--primary-light','rgba('+r+','+g+','+b+',.12)');
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--primary-hover','rgba('+r+','+g+','+b+',.85)');
  localStorage.setItem('kp_primary',color);
  kpToast('ڕەنگی سەرەکی گۆڕدرا ✓');
};

window.kpClearStorage=function(){
  ['kp_font_size','kp_grid_cols','kp_font','kp_srv_yt','kp_srv_vm',
   'kp_sub_color','kp_sub_size','kp_sub_bg','kp_dark','kp_anim',
   'kp_hover','kp_views','kp_date','kp_primary','kp_numstyle','kp_lazy'
  ].forEach(function(k){try{localStorage.removeItem(k);}catch(e){}});
  kpToast('هەموو ڕێکخستنەکان سڕایەوە...');
  setTimeout(function(){location.reload();},1500);
};
/* جێبەجێکردن لە بارکردنی پەڕە */
(function(){
  var primary=localStorage.getItem('kp_primary');
  if(primary){
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--primary',primary);
    var hex=primary.replace('#','');
    var r=parseInt(hex.substring(0,2),16),g=parseInt(hex.substring(2,4),16),b=parseInt(hex.substring(4,6),16);
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--primary-light','rgba('+r+','+g+','+b+',.12)');
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--primary-hover','rgba('+r+','+g+','+b+',.85)');
  }
  if(localStorage.getItem('kp_anim')==='0')document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--transition','0s');
  if(localStorage.getItem('kp_hover')==='0'){var sh=document.createElement('style');sh.id='kp-adv-hover-style';sh.textContent='.post-card:hover{transform:none!important;box-shadow:var(--shadow-md)!important}';document.head.appendChild(sh);}
  if(localStorage.getItem('kp_views')==='0'){var sv=document.createElement('style');sv.id='kp-adv-views-style';sv.textContent='.post-card-views,.kp-views{display:none!important}';document.head.appendChild(sv);}
  if(localStorage.getItem('kp_date')==='0'){var sd=document.createElement('style');sd.id='kp-adv-date-style';sd.textContent='.post-card-date,.kp-date,.post-date{display:none!important}';document.head.appendChild(sd);}
})();
/* نوێکردنەوەی toggle‌ەکان کاتی کرانەوەی مۆدال */
var _kpOrigShow=window.kpShowSettings;
window.kpShowSettings=function(){
  _kpOrigShow&&_kpOrigShow();
  var m={
    'kp-adv-anim':'kp_anim','kp-adv-hover':'kp_hover',
    'kp-adv-views':'kp_views','kp-adv-date':'kp_date','kp-adv-lazy':'kp_lazy'
  };
  Object.keys(m).forEach(function(id){
    var el=document.getElementById(id);
    if(el)el.checked=localStorage.getItem(m[id])!=='0';
  });
  var saved=localStorage.getItem('kp_primary');
  if(saved)document.querySelectorAll('.kp-color-dot').forEach(function(c){
    var a=c.dataset.color===saved;
    c.classList.toggle('active',a);
    c.style.outline=a?'2.5px solid var(--text-main)':'none';
    c.style.outlineOffset='2px';
  });
  var ns=localStorage.getItem('kp_numstyle')||'arabic';
  document.querySelectorAll('.kp-numstyle').forEach(function(c){c.classList.toggle('active',c.dataset.style===ns);});
};

})();

</script>

<!-- &#9552;&#9552; KP Notify Button JS &#9552;&#9552; -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
(function(){
  function kpNotifyUpdateUI(isSubscribed){
    var btn=document.getElementById('kp-notify-btn');
    var icon=document.getElementById('kp-notify-icon');
    if(!btn||!icon) return;
    if(isSubscribed){
      btn.classList.add('subscribed');
      btn.title='ئاگانامەکان چاڵاکە ✓';
      icon.className='fa-solid fa-bell';
      icon.style.animation='none';
    } else {
      btn.classList.remove('subscribed');
      btn.title='ئاگانامەکان چاڵاک بکە';
      icon.className='fa-solid fa-bell';
      icon.style.animation='';
    }
  }
  window.kpToggleNotify=function(){
    if(typeof OneSignal==='undefined'){
      window.OneSignalDeferred=window.OneSignalDeferred||[];
      window.OneSignalDeferred.push(function(os){
        os.Notifications.requestPermission();
      });
      return;
    }
    try{
      var os=window.OneSignal;
      var perm=os.Notifications.permission;
      if(perm==='denied'){
        alert('ئاگانامەکان لە براوزەرەکەتدا بڵۆک کراون.\nبۆ چاڵاک کردنەوەیان: Settings > Notifications > kuripak2026.blogspot.com > Allow');
        return;
      }
      if(perm!=='granted'){
        os.Notifications.requestPermission().then(function(){
          var sub=os.User&&os.User.PushSubscription&&os.User.PushSubscription.optedIn;
          kpNotifyUpdateUI(!!sub);
        });
      } else {
        // Toggle subscription
        var optedIn=os.User&&os.User.PushSubscription&&os.User.PushSubscription.optedIn;
        if(optedIn){
          os.User.PushSubscription.optOut().then(function(){ kpNotifyUpdateUI(false); });
        } else {
          os.User.PushSubscription.optIn().then(function(){ kpNotifyUpdateUI(true); });
        }
      }
    }catch(e){
      window.OneSignalDeferred=window.OneSignalDeferred||[];
      window.OneSignalDeferred.push(function(os){ os.Notifications.requestPermission(); });
    }
  };
  // ── دیاریکردنی حاڵەتی دوگمە دوای بارکردنی OneSignal ──
  window.OneSignalDeferred=window.OneSignalDeferred||[];
  window.OneSignalDeferred.push(function(os){
    try{
      var sub=os.User&&os.User.PushSubscription&&os.User.PushSubscription.optedIn;
      kpNotifyUpdateUI(!!sub);
      os.User.PushSubscription.addEventListener('change',function(ev){
        kpNotifyUpdateUI(!!(ev&&ev.current&&ev.current.optedIn));
      });
    }catch(e){}
  });
})();
//]]>
</script>
